Since sterilizing-filters are often used in the final manufacturing steps of a pharmaceutical production process, the effect of the filter on the final product should be evaluated. An extractable is any chemical component that is removed from a material by the application of an artificial or exaggerated condition (e.g., solvent, temperature, time). A leachable is a chemical component that migrates from a contact surface into a drug product or process fluid during storage or normal use conditions. These are typically a subset of extractables (19, 20).

        

Potential sources of extractables and leachables include, but are not limited to, membrane components (e.g., plasticizers, surfactants, antioxidants, residual solvents, device support layers), and device components (e.g., end caps, housings, cages, O-rings). Factors affecting leachables may include the chemical properties of the process stream, sterilization process, contact time, temperature, and volume-to-area ratios (21). Filtration of organic solutions may lead to higher levels of leachables than aqueous solutions.

        

Extractable data may be obtained from the filter manufacturer or may be generated by the filter user (see Section 6.5 for filter user-generated data). Filter manufacturers can use model streams to determine the extractable profiles under worst case conditions (22). Although an important component of filter validation, the level of extractables and leachables from most sterilizing-grade filters that can potentially enter the process stream is relatively low. Flushing the filters prior to use can further reduce these levels as demonstrated by flush curves measured by TOC or other tests for specific leachables (21).

        

Data should ideally include a comprehensive list of the compounds that could be leachables when the filter is used in the actual formulation under process conditions. The necessity to perform leachable study should be evaluated based on risk determined from extractable studies and risk to patient safety.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Extractables (可萃取物)：**在人為加強條件（強溶劑、高溫、長時間）下從材料中被萃取出來的化學物質。這是「最壞情況」的全面清單。

            

**Leachables (可溶出物)：**在正常使用或儲存條件下，從接觸表面遷移到藥品中的化學物質。通常是可萃取物的子集 -- 也就是說，在正常條件下實際會跑出來的量比極端條件下少很多。

            

**Volume-to-Area Ratio (體積面積比)：**製程液體體積與濾膜接觸面積的比值。比值越小（少量液體接觸大面積濾膜），單位體積中的可溶出物濃度可能越高。

            

**Flush Curve (沖洗曲線)：**以 TOC 或特定分析方法監測沖洗液中萃取物濃度隨沖洗量變化的趨勢。當曲線降至可接受水平時，即可停止預沖洗。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

Extractables 和 Leachables 的關係就像洗車：如果你用高壓水槍加清潔劑猛沖（極端條件 = extractables），車身上所有能被沖下來的東西都會下來 -- 灰塵、鳥糞、蠟層、甚至一點點漆。但如果只是下一場普通小雨（正常使用條件 = leachables），可能只會沖掉表面的灰塵。所以 leachables 通常是 extractables 的子集。但你做 extractables 測試的目的就是要先知道「最壞情況」，再來評估「正常情況」的風險。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**有機溶劑的特殊風險：**原文指出過濾有機溶液可能導致更高水平的可溶出物。這對使用有機溶劑的製程（如某些小分子藥物的最終過濾步驟）尤為重要。濾膜材質的選擇和 E&L 研究設計都需要特別考量。

            

**患者安全是最終考量：**是否需要執行可溶出物研究，最終取決於對患者安全的風險評估。即使可萃取物水平看起來很低，如果其中包含已知的致癌物或基因毒性物質，仍需進行詳細的可溶出物研究。這再次印證了決策層級中「無菌保證/患者安全」永遠排在第一位。

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Formula

            

**E&L 風險評估的關鍵變數：**

            

```

可溶出物風險 = f(萃取物種類, 接觸時間, 溫度,
                溶劑強度, 體積面積比, 滅菌方法)

實際可溶出物濃度 (估算) =
  萃取物總量 x 萃取效率因子 x (接觸時間/萃取時間)
  ÷ 藥品體積

其中：有機溶劑的萃取效率因子 > 水溶液的萃取效率因子
            
```

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼原文說「leachables are typically a subset of extractables」？在什麼罕見情況下，可能會出現不在 extractables 清單中的 leachables？

                
2. 你正在設計一個小批量生物製劑的除菌過濾步驟，批量只有 5L，但使用了標準 10 吋濾芯。從 volume-to-area ratio 的角度，你應該擔心什麼？如何緩解這個風險？

            

        

    

4.6.1 Chemical Compatibility

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

The chemical compatibility of the filter device must be evaluated to avoid potential filter damage or alteration and to avoid fluid contamination by either leachables or particulates. Filter manufacturers will have general chemical-compatibility guides based on the MoC and a range of standard chemicals. Since there may be numerous chemical interactions between filter device components and the process fluid or solvents, the typical chemical compatibility table provided by the filter manufacturer is commonly used as a starting point for further testing. More extensive testing should be performed by the end user to determine chemical compatibility of the filter device and process fluid under process conditions (see Section 6.0 for more details).

        

Chemical-compatibility testing should encompass the entire device and depends on the fluid, filtration temperature, and contact time. Additional studies should be performed by the filter user. Additional product-specific studies may be conducted by the filter vendor on request from the filter user to ensure there is no impact to product CQAs. Common chemical-compatibility tests include integrity test, tensile strength, nonvolatile residue (NVR), extractables, particulates, flow rate, optical or scanning electron microscopy (SEM), burst pressure and membrane/O-ring thickness (23). Use of a combination of tests is recommended since a single test might not be able to detect subtle incompatibilities.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Chemical Compatibility (化學相容性)：**濾膜及其所有組件（膜材、外殼、O-ring、支撐層等）與製程液體在實際操作條件下不發生有害化學反應的能力。不相容可能導致：

            

                
- 濾膜結構受損 → 細菌攔截失敗

                
- 萃取物/微粒增加 → 產品污染

                
- 完整性測試失敗 → 批次報廢

            

            

**Entire Device（整個裝置）：**強調不能只測試濾膜本身，還要包括 O-ring、外殼、端蓋等所有接觸零件。往往是非膜材組件（如 O-ring）最容易出現相容性問題。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

化學相容性測試就像在買新的保鮮盒裝酸性食物（如番茄醬、醋）之前：你不只需要知道盒體材質耐不耐酸，還要確認蓋子的矽膠密封圈不會被腐蝕、卡扣不會變脆斷裂。濾膜製造商的相容性表就像保鮮盒包裝上的「適用食材」列表 -- 它只是起點。如果你要裝的是一種特殊的辣椒醬（專屬藥品配方），你可能需要自己做實際測試才能放心。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**多測試方法組合的必要性：**原文明確建議使用「多種測試的組合」，因為單一測試可能無法檢測到微妙的不相容性。例如：

            

                
- 完整性測試可能通過，但 SEM 顯示膜表面已有微觀損傷

                
- 流速沒有變化，但 NVR（不揮發性殘留物）顯著增加，代表有物質溶出

                
- 拉伸強度下降表示材料正在降解，即使其他指標看起來正常

            

            

這就是為什麼化學相容性評估是一個綜合性的、多維度的評估過程。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼化學相容性測試需要在實際製程條件（溫度、接觸時間、流速）下進行，而不是只用室溫靜態浸泡？

                
2. 某客戶的藥品配方含有 20% 乙醇。從化學相容性的角度，你會特別關注濾器的哪些組件？為什麼？

            

        

    

4.7 Operational Ranges

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Manufacturers typically specify the maximum operational temperature, pressure, and sterilization temperature limits and provide water flow-rate data for their filters. Manufacturers provide maximum forward and reverse differential pressure limits at specific temperature conditions, incorporating adequate safety margins. This information may also reference limits at different temperatures, facilitating the selection of process flow rates, temperatures, and sterilization options compatible with the filter. Section 8.0 addresses selection and validation of sterilization options by the filter user.

        

Filter-system flow rate at a given differential pressure is a function of membrane polymer and structure type, pore size, housing inlet and outlet diameter, effective filter area, fluid temperature and viscosity. During the design of a process filtration system, these variables should be evaluated for compatibility with the operating limits of the filters and the filter area selected. Filter suppliers also test pressure-pulsation cycles to determine the mechanical stability of the filter device. However, care should be taken to avoid pressures exceeding the manufacturer's stated specifications of maximum allowable differential pressure at specified temperature ranges.

        

Note: There may be a distinction between the operational ranges with which a filter is generally suitable, and the "validated filtration parameters" for a sterilizing filtration unit operation, as defined in process-specific bacterial retention study validation in order to cover scale-down worst-case process conditions (see Section 6.0).

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Differential Pressure (差壓)：**濾膜上游與下游之間的壓力差。差壓太高可能損壞濾膜結構，導致完整性失敗；差壓太低則流速不足。製造商會提供在不同溫度下的最大允許差壓。

            

**Operational Range vs. Validated Parameters（操作範圍 vs. 驗證參數）：**這是一個關鍵區分 --

            

                
- **操作範圍：**製造商說「這個濾膜可以在 X 溫度、Y 壓力下使用」-- 這是通用的硬體極限

                
- **驗證參數：**你在自己的製程中，經過細菌攔截驗證後確認的實際可用參數範圍 -- 通常比操作範圍更窄

            

            

**Pressure-Pulsation Cycles (壓力脈動循環)：**模擬實際操作中壓力的波動變化（如泵浦造成的脈動），測試濾膜在反覆壓力變化下的機械穩定性。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

操作範圍和驗證參數的區別就像汽車的設計時速和你在特定道路上的安全駕駛速度：車廠說這輛車最高時速可達 250 km/h（操作範圍），但在你家附近的山路上，經過實際測試後，安全速度可能只有 80 km/h（驗證參數）。超過這個速度不一定會翻車，但你無法保證安全 -- 因為你只驗證到 80 km/h。同理，濾膜製造商的操作範圍是「硬體不會壞」的極限，但你的「除菌保證」只在你驗證過的參數範圍內有效。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**溫度與壓力的交互作用：**這是一個常被忽略的重點。最大允許差壓通常會隨溫度升高而降低。例如，某濾膜在 25°C 時最大差壓是 5 bar，但在 80°C 時可能只有 2.5 bar。如果你在高溫條件下過濾卻使用了常溫的壓力限制，可能會損壞濾膜。

            

**SIP（就地滅菌）的極端條件：**SIP 過程中的高溫（通常 121-134°C）和蒸汽壓力對濾膜是最嚴苛的考驗。滅菌溫度限制和操作溫度限制可能不同 -- 務必區分。

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Formula

            

**流速影響因素：**

            

```

Flow Rate = f(ΔP, A_eff, μ, T, d_pore, d_inlet/outlet)

其中：
  ΔP    = 差壓 (Differential Pressure)
  A_eff = 有效過濾面積 (EFA)
  μ     = 液體黏度 (隨溫度變化)
  T     = 溫度 (影響黏度和最大差壓)
  d_pore = 孔徑大小
  d_inlet/outlet = 外殼進出口口徑

注意：溫度升高 → 黏度降低 → 流速增加
      但同時 → 最大允許差壓降低 → 操作窗口縮小
            
```

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 你的製程在 60°C 下過濾高黏度蛋白質溶液。在選擇操作壓力時，你需要考量哪些互相矛盾的因素？如何找到最佳操作點？

                
2. 為什麼原文特別提到「forward and reverse differential pressure limits」？在什麼情況下會出現反向差壓？這對濾膜完整性有什麼風險？

            

        

    

4.8 Shelf Life and Shipping Studies

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Filter manufacturers will validate packaging and shipping of the filters according to industry standards to ensure that the products can withstand common transport hazards (24). In addition, filter manufacturers will establish shelf-life recommendations based on product stability under defined conditions, which will be valid if the filter is stored and handled properly. These recommendations can be used by the filter user to establish expiration dates or use-by dates.

        

Filters that are sterilized via gamma or x-ray irradiation will have expiration dates due to the sterility claim associated with the sterilization method.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Shelf Life (保存期限)：**濾膜在製造商建議的儲存條件下，能維持其品質特性和性能規格的期間。超過保存期限的濾膜不應使用於藥品製造。

            

**Sterility Claim (無菌聲明)：**經 gamma 或 x-ray 輻射滅菌的濾器具有「預滅菌」聲明，此聲明有時效性 -- 因為包裝材料會隨時間老化，可能喪失無菌屏障功能。因此這類濾器一定有明確的有效期。

            

**Shipping Validation (運輸驗證)：**依據 ISTA 或 ASTM D4169 等標準，模擬運輸過程中的振動、跌落、壓縮等風險，確保濾器在送達使用者手中時仍完好無損。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

濾器的保存期限管理就像超市食品的有效期：牛奶（經輻射滅菌的囊式濾器）有明確的有效日期，過期就不能喝；罐頭（未預滅菌的不鏽鋼濾芯）保存期限較長，但仍然有限制。而運輸驗證就像網購易碎品的包裝測試 -- 供應商必須確保產品能承受快遞運輸過程中的各種碰撞和擠壓，安全送到你手上。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**CDMO 庫存管理的注意事項：**

            

                
- **先進先出 (FIFO)：**嚴格執行物料輪替，避免過期報廢

                
- **儲存條件監控：**溫度、濕度超出範圍可能加速材料老化，縮短實際保存期限

                
- **收貨檢驗：**進貨時應檢查包裝完整性，確認運輸過程中未受損

                
- **輻射滅菌濾器的特殊管理：**這些濾器的有效期通常比未滅菌濾器短，需要更積極的庫存管理

            

            

在多產品 CDMO 中，不同客戶可能指定不同品牌/型號的濾器，庫存品項繁多 -- 過期報廢是實際且常見的成本浪費。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**供應鏈策略：**COVID-19 疫情期間，全球單次使用組件供應鏈嚴重中斷，許多藥廠面臨濾器缺貨危機。建議 CDMO 採取：

            

                
1. 建立安全庫存（但要平衡過期風險）

                
2. 驗證至少兩個供應商的替代濾器

                
3. 與供應商建立長期合約和優先供貨協議

                
4. 考慮 consignment stock（寄售庫存）模式降低資金占壓

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果一批 gamma 滅菌的囊式濾器在倉庫中被發現儲存溫度曾超過建議上限（但仍在保存期限內），你會如何處理？可以直接使用嗎？

                
2. 從供應鏈韌性 (supply chain resilience) 的角度，使用 SUS 濾器系統相比傳統不鏽鋼系統有什麼額外的風險？如何緩解？

            

        

    

    

### 本節重點回顧 Section Summary

    

        
- **責任劃分明確：**濾膜製造商負責確效 (Q) 和批次放行 (L)，使用者負責製程驗證 (V) 和額外評估 (E)。Table 4.1-1 是最重要的責任分工參考表。

        
- **濾膜設計影響性能：**褶皺密度決定 EFA（有效過濾面積），進而影響流速和處理量。Scale-up 時須注意 PD 階段與量產階段濾器幾何設計的差異。

        
- **SUS 的雙面性：**一次性使用系統消除了清洗驗證和交叉污染風險，但帶來了供應鏈依賴、廢棄物管理和 E&L 評估的新挑戰。

        
- **E&L 是層層遞進的：**先做可萃取物 (Extractables) 研究建立最壞情況基線，再根據風險評估決定是否需要可溶出物 (Leachables) 研究。預沖洗可有效降低兩者的水平。

        
- **化學相容性需全面評估：**必須測試整個裝置（不只是膜材），使用多種測試方法的組合，在實際製程條件下進行。

        
- **操作範圍 ≠ 驗證參數：**製造商的操作範圍是硬體極限，使用者的驗證參數（來自細菌攔截驗證）才是除菌保證的依據。

        
- **保存期限管理不可忽視：**尤其是 gamma/x-ray 滅菌的濾器有明確有效期，需嚴格執行 FIFO 和儲存條件監控。

        
- **決策層級再次確認：**所有選擇（材質、型式、供應商）最終都回歸到：無菌保證 > 產品 CQA > 商業彈性的優先順序。

## Section 5: Process Design 製程設計 (p23-p38)

# Section 5.0 Filtration Process Design, Usage, and Handling Considerations (Part A)

    

過濾製程設計、使用與操作考量（第一部分：5.0 - 5.4.1）

    

PDA Technical Report No. 26 (Revised 2025) — Sterilizing Filtration of Liquids | p23 - p31

    

### 本章學習目標

    

        
- 理解除菌過濾製程設計（Filtration Process Design）的整體架構，掌握 FDA 製程驗證三階段與 ICH Q8 設計空間的核心理念

        
- 學會如何評估產品特性與濾膜相容性（Product Properties and Filter Compatibility），包含化學相容性、物理特性與吸附效應

        
- 掌握設計空間（Design Space）的定義方法，了解影響過濾操作範圍的關鍵因子（溫度、體積、流速、壓力、時間等）

        
- 理解流量特性（Flow Characteristics）、入口/差壓（Inlet/Differential Pressure）、過濾溫度（Temperature）、過濾時間（Filtration Time）的相互關係與製程影響

        
- 掌握濾膜通量與最大體積（Filter Throughput and Maximum Volume）的評估方法及影響因子

        
- 理解縮小規模系統（Scale-Down Systems）與小規模裝置測試（Small Scale Device Testing）的原理、方法與放大注意事項

    

5.0 Filtration Process Design, Usage, and Handling Considerations

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

According to the FDA's Guidance for Industry: Process Validation: General Principles and Practices (Revision 1), quality, efficacy, and safety must be built into the product and cannot be tested at the end of the manufacturing process. This concept is especially important for many sterilizing filtration operations, as the filter often represents the final microbial control barrier prior to patient dosing (25). This guidance document outlines three stages of process validation: Stage 1-Process Design, Stage 2-Process Qualification, and Stage 3-Continued Process Verification. Section 5.0 focuses on the process design aspects, and Section 6.0 focuses on the process-specific validation requirements for a sterilizing filtration process. Continued process verification is generally out of scope in this document and is covered in other guidance documents. The process design methodology discussed here is consistent with the principles of the International Council for Harmonization (ICH) Quality Guideline (Q8): Pharmaceutical Development, which is to first evaluate the design space, then develop a control strategy (8).

        

Membrane filters are used for multiple applications within the pharmaceutical industry and therefore, membrane filter types, designs and configurations are as varied as their applications. This chapter will focus on the process design and usage of sterilizing filters for the removal of microorganisms in pharmaceutical processing. Many of these design principles will also apply to the use of sterilizing-grade filters in locations other than the final sterilizing barrier for the control of bioburden, although those use cases have significantly reduced risk to product quality and may not require the same level of validation and controls to be applied (26).

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**製程驗證三階段（Three Stages of Process Validation）：**

            

                
- **Stage 1 - Process Design（製程設計）：**透過開發活動，定義製程的商業化製造條件。本章（5.0）正是聚焦於此。

                
- **Stage 2 - Process Qualification（製程確認）：**在實際製造環境中驗證設計的製程能夠可重複地運作。Section 6.0 涵蓋此內容。

                
- **Stage 3 - Continued Process Verification（持續製程確認）：**持續監控，確保製程維持在受控狀態。

            

            

**ICH Q8 設計空間（Design Space）：**先定義出操作空間的邊界，再建立控制策略 (Control Strategy)，確保在空間內的任何操作條件都能穩定產出合格產品。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像你是一位大廚要開新餐廳。你不會等食物端上桌後才檢查好不好吃（那就是「事後檢驗」）。正確做法是：

            

                
- **Stage 1（設計）：**先在實驗廚房研發菜單，確定食材、溫度、時間的最佳範圍

                
- **Stage 2（確認）：**在正式廚房依配方試做，確認出品一致

                
- **Stage 3（監控）：**開業後持續品管，確保每道菜的品質不走味

            

            

除菌過濾就像餐廳最後一道食安關卡 -- 如果你的食材本身已經有問題，再好的過濾也無法完全補救。「品質內建」的概念就是從源頭把關。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**濾膜是最後的微生物控制屏障：**在無菌充填製程中，除菌濾膜（Sterilizing Filter）往往是產品給予病患前的最後一道防線。這意味著過濾失敗 = 直接影響病患安全，沒有後續補救手段。

            

**非最終屏障的應用：**除菌級濾膜也可用於中間製程的 Bioburden（生物負荷）控制，這些應用的風險較低，驗證要求可以適度簡化。但「可以簡化」不代表「可以忽略」。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 情境：**作為 CDMO，你可能同時為多個客戶代工不同產品，每個產品的除菌過濾製程都需要獨立的 Stage 1 設計。即使使用相同型號的濾膜，不同產品的化學特性、粒子負荷、溫度要求都不同，設計空間必須個別建立。這是合規的基本要求，也是客戶稽核時的重點關注項目。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. FDA 製程驗證三階段中，為什麼 Stage 1（製程設計）必須在 Stage 2（製程確認）之前完成？如果跳過會有什麼後果？

                
2. 為什麼 TR26 強調除菌濾膜是「final microbial control barrier」？在你的工廠中，是否有其他微生物控制措施可以作為後備？

            

        

    

5.1 Process Design: Design Space Evaluation

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

An initial evaluation of the design space for a sterilizing-filtration operation will generally encompass a survey of the product properties, compatibility and required operational ranges used in the process.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Design Space（設計空間）：**根據 ICH Q8 的定義，設計空間是「經證明能提供品質保證的多維度組合與交互作用」。在除菌過濾中，這意味著你必須定義出溫度、壓力、流速、體積、時間等參數的安全操作範圍。

            

設計空間的三大要素評估順序：

            

                
1. **產品特性（Product Properties）：**了解你要過濾什麼

                
2. **相容性（Compatibility）：**確認產品與濾膜系統能和平共處

                
3. **操作範圍（Operational Ranges）：**定義每個參數的上下限

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

設計空間就像開車時的安全駕駛範圍：你的車有速限（最大壓力），有最低油溫才能正常運轉（最低溫度），輪胎有最大承載量（最大體積），油箱有容量限制（過濾時間）。只有在所有這些參數同時落在安全範圍內，你才能安全到達目的地。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

注意這裡說的是「初步評估」（initial evaluation），暗示設計空間的建立是一個迭代過程 -- 隨著你獲得更多製程知識，空間會不斷精煉。不要期望一次就能完美定義所有範圍。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. ICH Q8 提出的「設計空間」概念如何應用到除菌過濾？與傳統的單一操作條件驗證有何不同？

                
2. 為什麼評估順序是產品特性 → 相容性 → 操作範圍？能否顛倒順序？

            

        

    

5.1.1 Product Properties and Filter Compatibility

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

A good first step in the design of a sterilizing-filtration process is to evaluate the solution that needs to be sterilized and how it will interact with the filtration system. A thorough evaluation of the properties of the filtrate will guide in the selection of a filtration membrane and housing system that can withstand chemical stress such as solvents, strongly basic or acidic media, and high-ionic strengths. After performing this type of analysis, it can allow the user to select filtration systems that are appropriate for the application.

        

For the second step of the compatibility analysis, an evaluation of the physical properties of the process fluid and intended processing parameters should be carried out. Characteristics such as the fluid temperature range, particulate load, and viscosity can also affect the filter membrane and filtration system selection. The system must be able to handle the mechanical stresses placed on it and remain integral for the duration of the filtration process. Since there may be numerous chemical interactions between filter device/SUS components and the process fluid or solvents, the typical chemical compatibility table provided by the filter manufacturer is commonly used as a starting point for filter selection.

        

Another dimension of filter compatibility to consider is adsorption of components from the process stream. Adsorption is a mechanism of product binding to the membrane or product contacting materials, which may affect the product composition and concentration. Potential adsorption of product components to the filter and other components of the filtration system (e.g., bags, connectors, tubing) must be considered independently. Considerations should include membrane type, MoC used throughout the filtration system, hardware, and support materials. Flow rate, product concentration, contact time, process fluid components, temperature and pH can also affect the level of adsorption.

        

In instances where elevated adsorption occurs in the beginning of the filtration process but levels off during filtration, the filtered volume could be pooled to achieve the specified product composition. During PD, adsorption tests are typically performed at small scale and confirmed at large scale. These tests can also be used to establish potential pretreatment options (e.g., buffer flush, soaking), necessary process parameter options or membrane polymer choices. Elevated levels of nonspecific product adsorption on the filter membrane can result in accelerated filter-fouling and performance degradation that would need to be studied as part of filter-sizing studies.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**相容性分析的兩步驟：**

            

**第一步 -- 化學相容性（Chemical Compatibility）：**

            

                
- 評估溶液的化學特性（溶劑、酸鹼度、離子強度）

                
- 確認濾膜材質和外殼（Housing）能否承受這些化學環境

                
- 起點：濾膜製造商的化學相容性表

            

            

**第二步 -- 物理相容性（Physical Compatibility）：**

            

                
- 評估溫度範圍、粒子負荷、黏度

                
- 確認系統能承受機械應力並在整個過濾過程維持完整性

            

            

**Adsorption（吸附）：**產品成分與濾膜或系統材料結合的現象。這不是過濾的目的，而是副作用。吸附可能導致：

            

                
- 產品濃度降低 -- 尤其對高價值生物製劑影響巨大

                
- 產品組成改變 -- 某些成分被選擇性吸附

                
- 濾膜堵塞加速 -- 吸附物累積導致 Fouling（堵塞）

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像你要用一個新的水壺泡茶。你需要考慮：

            

                
- **化學相容性：**這個水壺材質能不能承受熱水？會不會被茶的單寧酸腐蝕？就像確認濾膜能否承受你的製程液體

                
- **物理相容性：**水壺夠大嗎？能承受高溫嗎？就像確認過濾系統能處理你的溫度和體積

                
- **吸附問題：**新水壺會不會吸走茶的香氣或顏色？就像濾膜會吸附某些藥物成分。前幾壺泡出來的茶味道不對，但泡久了就穩定了 -- 這就是「初期吸附高，後來趨於平穩」的現象

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**MoC（Materials of Construction，建構材料）：**吸附評估不能只看濾膜！整個過濾系統的所有接觸面（bags、connectors、tubing）都可能吸附產品成分，必須個別評估。

            

**預處理選項：**Buffer flush（緩衝液沖洗）或 soaking（浸泡）可以「飽和」濾膜的吸附位點，減少後續過濾時的產品損失。對於高價值的生物製劑，這是常見的實務做法。

            

**Filter-Fouling（濾膜堵塞）：**非特異性吸附不僅影響產品收率，還會加速濾膜堵塞，直接影響過濾性能和 Filter Sizing（濾膜規格選擇）。

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Formula

            

**吸附率估算概念：**

            

```

Adsorption Rate = (C_feed - C_filtrate) / C_feed x 100%

其中：
  C_feed = 進料端產品濃度
  C_filtrate = 濾液端產品濃度

若 Adsorption Rate > 可接受範圍：
  → 考慮 Buffer flush 預處理
  → 評估替代濾膜材質
  → 調整過濾體積以池化稀釋
            
```

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 情境：**一家 CDMO 接到新客戶的單株抗體（mAb）產品代工需求。在除菌過濾製程設計階段，你發現該 mAb 的等電點（pI）接近製程 pH，導致蛋白質在 PVDF 膜上的吸附率高達 15%。

            

應對策略：(1) 切換至 PES 膜材測試吸附率 (2) 進行 buffer flush 預處理降低初始吸附 (3) 評估池化策略是否可行 (4) 計算吸附導致的產品損失成本，與更換濾膜的成本做比較。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼化學相容性評估要在物理相容性之前？如果順序顛倒，可能遇到什麼問題？

                
2. 對於一個高濃度蛋白質藥物，你預期在過濾初期和後期的吸附行為會有什麼不同？這對生產操作有什麼影響？

                
3. 除了濾膜本身，還有哪些過濾系統組件需要評估吸附風險？列舉至少三個。

            

        

    

5.1.2 Defining the Design Space and Operational Ranges

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Knowledge of the desired at-scale process prospectively allows setting ranges to be studied during the development of the filtration process. For example, a survey of the compounding process and the maximum and minimum volumes that will flow through the filter during the sterilizing filtration process can create an important set of operational ranges that the filter must be able to process. In addition, a subset of these parameters will define ranges that need to be validated later (see Section 6.3). While some parameters can be difficult to know during the initial PD exercise, it can be useful to evaluate the potential market demands for the product and maximum expected batch volume. This will potentially reduce the need for additional development and revalidation of the sterilizing-filtration process as the conditions change over the product lifecycle. Table 5.1.2-1 shows a list of potential factors to consider during the process design phase that can help determine operational ranges to study.

        

        
            Table 5.1.2-1 Factors to Consider When Developing Operational Ranges for Study During Sterilizing-Filtration Process Design and Development
            
                
                
                
            
| Factor | Extent | Rationale |
| --- | --- | --- |
            
                
                
                
            
| Temperature | Refrigerated to Warmed | Dependent on product quality effects and physical property optimization, can affect filter differential pressures and flow rate due to viscosity differences and also microbial growth rates |
            
                
                
                
            
| Total Product Volume | Minimum and Maximum | Sets limits for bacterial retention study validation and allows proper filter sizing |
            
                
                
                
            
| Flow Rate | Zero to Maximum Expected | Flow rate dependent on application, e.g., in line with sterile filling machine or bulk filtration |
            
                
                
                
            
| Differential Pressure | Minimum to Maximum | Requires appropriate development studies to determine pressure/flow rate relationship; reasonable maximum differential pressure should be defined based on expected conditions as well as a minimum expected to aid, for example, in detection of filter installation errors |
            
                
                
                
            
| Filtration Time | Maximum | Dependent on the processing time required, determines how long the process will take, including process setup and any necessary process stops |
            
                
                
                
            
| Product Contact Time | Maximum | Extended contact time may impact product compatibility, membrane fouling, or filter integrity |
            
                
                
                
            
| Driving Force | Pulsatile and/or Constant Pressure | Determines what type of pump or driving force will be used in the commercial setting; certain filters may be used in more than one manufacturing setup |
            
                
                
                
            
| Configuration | Single or Redundant Filter Setup or Multiple Filter Setup | Knowledge of physical size constraints for the filter may necessitate the use of multiple filters; site, business or procedural factors may also require the use of redundant filtration; and knowing this up front will aid in the design of the filtration process |
        

        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**前瞻性設計（Prospective Design）：**TR26 強調在設計階段就要預見商業化規模的需求。不要只看現在的臨床批量，要考慮未來市場需求可能帶來的最大批量。這樣做的好處是避免日後因批量放大而需要重新驗證（Revalidation）。

            

**Table 5.1.2-1 八大設計因子：**

            

                
- **溫度（Temperature）：**從冷藏到加溫，影響黏度、流速和微生物生長

                
- **總產品體積（Total Product Volume）：**最小到最大，決定細菌截留驗證範圍和濾膜尺寸

                
- **流速（Flow Rate）：**零到最大預期值，取決於應用場景

                
- **差壓（Differential Pressure）：**最小到最大，需研究壓力與流速的關係

                
- **過濾時間（Filtration Time）：**最大值，包含製程設置和中斷時間

                
- **產品接觸時間（Product Contact Time）：**最大值，影響相容性和完整性

                
- **驅動力（Driving Force）：**脈動或恆壓，決定泵浦類型

                
- **配置（Configuration）：**單一或冗餘/多重濾膜，考量物理空間和風險管理

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

定義設計空間就像規劃高速公路。你不只考慮今天的車流量，還要預測未來 20 年的交通需求。如果只按現在的車流量設計雙線道，五年後車流量翻倍時就得重新施工擴建（= 重新驗證）。但如果一開始就預留四線道的空間（= 涵蓋未來最大批量），即使初期有些「多餘」，長期來看卻省下大量重建成本。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**最小差壓也很重要：**注意 Table 中「Differential Pressure」的範圍包含最小值。設定合理的最小差壓可以幫助偵測濾膜安裝錯誤 -- 如果過濾時壓差異常低，可能表示濾膜沒有正確安裝或存在旁路（bypass）。

            

**Product Contact Time vs Filtration Time：**這是兩個不同的概念。過濾時間是實際過濾的持續時間；產品接觸時間包含了製程等待時間、中斷時間等。後者通常更長，且是驗證的最差情境。

            

**Configuration 決策：**冗餘過濾（Redundant Filtration）在某些監管轄區可能是要求，而非選項。提前在設計空間中納入，避免後期被動修改。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 情境：**你的工廠目前為客戶生產 100L 批量的注射劑，但客戶的商業化計畫預計批量將擴展到 500L。如果你在設計空間中只驗證到 150L，當客戶需求增長時就必須重新進行細菌截留驗證和製程驗證，耗時 3-6 個月。但如果一開始就將設計空間擴展到 600L（含安全餘量），雖然初期研發成本多 20%，但可以避免未來的重新驗證，為公司節省大量時間和成本。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼 Table 5.1.2-1 中的「Flow Rate」範圍從「Zero」開始？在什麼情境下流速為零？

                
2. 「Driving Force」中提到 pulsatile（脈動）和 constant pressure（恆壓）兩種模式，各適用於什麼情境？為什麼這會影響設計空間？

                
3. 如果你是 CDMO 的製程開發人員，你會如何說服管理層在初期多投入資源建立更寬廣的設計空間？請用商業語言描述投資報酬率。

            

        

    

5.2 Flow Characteristics

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Flow-performance criteria during a filtration operation can include parameters such as flow rate, total throughput, thermal and mechanical resistance, and nonspecific adsorption. A filter's EFA is used in calculations for scaling filter performance, determining extractables levels, reporting flow rates (i.e., flux), and assuring of bacterial retention. Since applications vary, desired filter-performance characteristics also vary. For example, since buffers widely utilized in purification processes are nonfouling, the optimum filter may be one with the highest flow rate; for solutions that may contain foulants, such as media, the optimum filter may be one with the highest filtration capacity for that solution. Optimizing the filter to the process requires determination of critical and key operational parameters and performance requirements.

        

Filter flow rate is affected by such parameters as the EFA, membrane porosity, pore size, thickness and area, differential pressure, flow path design, fluid viscosity, and temperature. Table 5.2-1 shows the relationships between flow rate and a common list of process parameters.

        

        
            Table 5.2-1 Common Factors Affecting Flow Rate
            
                
                
            
| Higher Flow Rate | Lower Flow Rate |
| --- | --- |
            
                
                
            
| High Porosity/Greater Void Volume | Low Porosity/Lesser Void Volume |
            
                
                
            
| Large Pore Size | Small Pore Size |
            
                
                
            
| Thin Membrane (less hydraulic resistance) | Thick Membrane (greater hydraulic resistance) |
            
                
                
            
| Large Effective Filtration Area (EFA) | Low Effective Filtration Area (EFA) |
            
                
                
            
| High Differential Pressure (fluid force) | Low Differential Pressure |
            
                
                
            
| Straight Flow Path | Tortuous Flow Path |
            
                
                
            
| Low Viscosity | High Viscosity |
            
                
                
            
| High Temperature | Low Temperature |
        

        

        

Most of these parameters are governed by membrane and filter designs or particular fluid properties. The primary parameter is the differential pressure that is, the difference between inlet (feed side) and outlet (filtrate side) pressure. The differential pressure can be adjusted within the filter manufacturer supplied maximum temperature/pressure ranges to achieve the desired process flow rates. Studying the required pressure and flow rate ranges using scale-down membrane areas with the actual product stream is further elaborated in Section 5.4.1. It is important to understand this information thoroughly to determine the ranges that will be challenged during the validation activities (see Section 6.8).

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**EFA（Effective Filtration Area，有效過濾面積）：**這是過濾科學中最核心的參數之一。EFA 是濾膜實際參與過濾的表面積，是放大（Scale-up）和縮小（Scale-down）計算的基礎。

            

**Flux（通量）：**單位面積的流速，通常以 L/m²/hr 表示。這是比較不同尺寸濾膜性能的標準化指標。

            

**Table 5.2-1 的邏輯：**流速受八個因素影響，其中大部分由濾膜設計和液體性質決定。在實際操作中，你能直接控制的主要是差壓（Differential Pressure）-- 這就是為什麼它是「最關鍵的可調參數」。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

理解流速就像理解水龍頭出水。想像你家的水管：

            

                
- **孔隙大小（Pore Size）= 水管口徑：**管子越粗，水流越大

                
- **差壓（ΔP）= 水壓：**打開水壓開關，水流更大

                
- **黏度（Viscosity）= 水 vs 蜂蜜：**蜂蜜流得慢，需要更大壓力才能推動

                
- **膜厚度 = 水管長度：**管子越長，阻力越大

                
- **EFA = 多少條水管同時開：**開越多條，總流量越大

            

            

在所有這些因素中，你最容易調節的就是「水壓」（差壓），其他因素在你選定濾膜和液體後就固定了。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**不同應用有不同最佳化目標：**

            

                
- **緩衝液等非堵塞性流體：**最佳化目標 = 最大流速 → 選高通量濾膜

                
- **培養基等含污染物流體：**最佳化目標 = 最大通量（容量）→ 選高容量濾膜

            

            

同一支濾膜不一定同時是「最快」和「最能裝」的 -- 這需要根據應用場景做取捨。

            

**連結驗證：**本節的流速範圍研究結果，最終將用來定義 Section 6.8 中驗證活動的挑戰範圍。設計階段定義得越清楚，驗證活動就越精準高效。

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Formula

            

**基本流量關係（達西定律簡化版）：**

            

```

Q = (ΔP x A x K) / (μ x L)

其中：
  Q = 流量 (Flow Rate)
  ΔP = 差壓 (Differential Pressure)
  A = 有效過濾面積 (EFA)
  K = 膜滲透係數 (Membrane Permeability)
  μ = 流體黏度 (Viscosity)
  L = 膜厚度 (Membrane Thickness)

Flux = Q / A = (ΔP x K) / (μ x L)

放大計算基礎：
  Q_large / Q_small = EFA_large / EFA_small
  （在相同 ΔP、溫度條件下）
            
```

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. Table 5.2-1 中的八個因素，哪些是操作人員可以控制的？哪些在選定濾膜後就固定了？

                
2. 為什麼「Tortuous Flow Path」（彎曲流路）會降低流速？但它對細菌截留有什麼影響？

                
3. 一位同事建議「既然壓力越高流速越快，那就把壓力開到最大」。這個建議有什麼風險？

            

        

    

5.2.1 Inlet and Differential Pressure

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

From the filtration curves it can be determined that increasing the pressure across the membrane will result in an increased flow rate under most processing conditions, which is an important variable to control during the sterilizing-filtration process. There are two important ways to specify the pressure: Differential pressure (ΔP) is the difference in pressure between the upstream (inlet) and downstream (effluent) sides of the filter, while inlet pressure is the pressure measured directly on the inlet side of the filter. To determine the differential pressure, the inlet pressure must be measured using a pressure gauge or sensor. When appropriate, outlet pressure may be assumed to be atmospheric (e.g., a vented downstream vessel). If the outlet pressure is higher than the atmospheric pressure (e.g., when the fluid is transferred into a pressurized or unvented system or if the flow rate causes a significant pressure drop downstream of the filter) either the outlet pressure must be measured, or assume that the inlet pressure represents a worst-case upper limit on the true differential pressure.

        

Depending on the flow regime and the safety factor to the validated maximum pressure it may be important to monitor the inlet or differential pressure of the filtration system (see Section 6.8). Increasing differential pressure at a constant flow rate is indicative of filter fouling, and detection may be important for certain types of process streams that are susceptible to fouling behavior.

        

Many modern filtration systems are driven by peristaltic pumps, especially in the case of SUS. As peristaltic pumps are a type of positive displacement pump, the flow rate can be easily controlled (correlated with pump revolutions per minute (RPM) and defined tubing diameter) without needing to worry about cleaning internal pump components or tubing systems; this adds a degree of safety and convenience to many filtration process designs. On the other hand, filtration can also be performed by pressurizing the system, managed by a pressure control valve, which avoids the need of a pump system. In most final sterilizing-filtration systems, the process stream is nonfouling and the filtration pressure remains relatively consistent over time. With proper system design and appropriate safety factors, constant flow rate or pressure filtration setups can operate in pressure regimes well below validated filter pressure limits. Some form of pressure control or monitoring may be an expectation of certain health authorities, even for pump-driven sterilization filtration processes that do not exhibit significant fouling.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Differential Pressure (ΔP，差壓) vs Inlet Pressure（入口壓力）：**

            

                
- **ΔP = P_inlet - P_outlet：**真正驅動液體通過濾膜的力。這才是影響過濾性能的核心參數。

                
- **Inlet Pressure：**只測量進料側的壓力。當出口為大氣壓（如排入開放容器）時，Inlet Pressure ≈ ΔP。

                
- 但如果出口端是加壓系統（如密封的儲槽），你必須同時測量出口壓力才能算出真正的 ΔP。

            

            

**Filter Fouling 指標：**在恆流速操作下，差壓逐漸上升 = 濾膜正在堵塞。這是一個重要的製程監控信號。

            

**兩種驅動模式：**

            

                
- **泵驅動（Pump-driven）：**蠕動泵（Peristaltic Pump）控制流速，壓力隨阻力變化

                
- **壓力驅動（Pressure-driven）：**壓力控制閥維持恆壓，流速隨阻力變化

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

差壓和入口壓力的差別，就像水塔供水：

            

                
- **入口壓力 = 水塔的水壓：**你可以在水表上讀到

                
- **出口壓力 = 你家樓層的水壓：**住在一樓幾乎是零，住在十樓就有明顯的背壓

                
- **差壓 = 真正推動水流的力：**如果水塔壓力 5 bar，你家背壓 2 bar，真正驅動水流的只有 3 bar

            

            

如果你只看水塔壓力就說「水壓很夠」，但忽略了你家背壓很高，實際水流可能很小。同樣地，只看 Inlet Pressure 可能會高估實際的過濾驅動力。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**蠕動泵（Peristaltic Pump）在一次性使用系統（SUS）中的優勢：**

            

                
- 無需清洗內部零件（流體只接觸管路，不接觸泵機構）

                
- 流速與轉速（RPM）和管徑直接相關，容易控制

                
- 非常適合一次性使用系統的理念

            

            

**監管期望：**即使是使用蠕動泵的恆流速系統，某些衛生主管機關仍然可能要求進行壓力監控。這意味著壓力感測器/壓力錶應該被視為標準配備，而非可選項。

            

**安全餘量原則：**適當的系統設計應確保操作壓力遠低於驗證的最大壓力限值，留有充足的安全裕度。

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Formula

            

```

差壓計算：
  ΔP = P_inlet - P_outlet

情境一：出口排入開放容器（vented vessel）
  P_outlet ≈ 大氣壓（1 atm）
  ΔP ≈ P_inlet - 1 atm

情境二：出口排入加壓系統
  P_outlet = 須實測
  ΔP = P_inlet - P_outlet（實測值）

情境三：無法測量出口壓力時
  假設 P_inlet = ΔP（最差情境上限）
  → 這是保守估算，確保不超過驗證壓力
            
```

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 情境：**你的無菌充填線使用蠕動泵驅動的一次性過濾系統。泵設定在固定 RPM，正常操作壓力約 1.2 bar。某次生產時，操作員注意到壓力已上升到 1.8 bar，但流速維持不變。

            

這代表什麼？ -- 濾膜正在堵塞（fouling）。雖然流速還正常，但如果壓力持續上升到接近驗證上限（例如 2.5 bar），就必須停止並更換濾膜。這就是差壓監控的價值：它能在問題影響產品品質之前提供預警。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 在什麼情況下，Inlet Pressure 不等於 Differential Pressure？請舉出你工廠中的實例。

                
2. 蠕動泵驅動系統和壓力驅動系統各有什麼優缺點？對於 CDMO 來說，你會如何選擇？

                
3. 為什麼在恆流速操作下，差壓上升是 filter fouling 的指標？如果是恆壓操作，fouling 的指標會是什麼？

            

        

    

5.2.2 Filtration Process Temperature

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Process temperature has a variety of effects on the filter and fluid stream. Elevated temperatures reduce the maximum allowable differential pressure due to the strength of the mechanical structure of the filter. Pressure limits may vary between forward-and-reverse flow directions, based on filter structure (reverse flow often being considered worst-case). Pressure limits at specific process temperatures may be listed by the filter manufacturer in the qualification documentation of the particular filter type. Figure 5.2.2-1 depicts an example of the relationship between process temperature and maximum differential pressure, that is, the higher the process temperature, the lower the pressure resistance of a filter. Under elevated temperature conditions, filter users should evaluate the risk factors, and if necessary, monitor process parameters carefully.

        

In addition to affecting differential-pressure capabilities, higher process temperatures could result in elevated leachables or chemical incompatibilities. Consideration should also be given to temperature, as some polymeric membranes are sensitive to hydrolytic and oxidative alterations by heat.

        

Higher temperatures reduce fluid viscosity and increase the flow rate through the filter for most Newtonian fluids. Higher viscosities could also result in the need for higher differential pressures to achieve a required flow rate. These elevated differential pressures correspondingly require increased monitoring of flow rate and/or differential pressure to avoid exceeding the rated pressure conditions.

        

Figure 5.2.2-1 Example of Filter Pressure/Temperature Resistance  
(Figure not available in text extraction — refer to original TR26 document p28)

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**溫度對過濾系統的三重影響：**

            

                
1. **機械強度降低：**溫度升高 → 濾膜材料軟化 → 最大承受壓力下降。這是一個反比關係：溫度越高，允許的最大差壓越低。

                
2. **可溶出物（Leachables）增加：**高溫促進濾膜材料中化學物質的溶出，可能影響產品品質和安全性。

                
3. **流體黏度降低：**溫度升高 → 黏度降低 → 流速增加。對於牛頓流體（Newtonian Fluids），這是正面效果。

            

            

**正向 vs 反向流動：**壓力限值在正向和反向流動可能不同。反向流動通常被視為最差情境，因為濾膜結構設計通常是針對正向流動最佳化的。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

溫度對濾膜的影響就像天氣對橡皮筋的影響：

            

                
- **低溫：**橡皮筋硬但結實，能承受大力拉扯（高壓力）

                
- **高溫：**橡皮筋軟化，容易被拉斷（低壓力就可能損壞）

                
- **流體黏度：**就像蜂蜜加熱後變稀一樣 -- 同樣的壓力下流動更快

            

            

但這裡有一個矛盾：高溫雖然讓液體更容易流動（好事），卻也讓濾膜變脆弱（壞事）。所以操作溫度需要在兩者之間找到平衡。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**溫度-壓力的反比關係：**Figure 5.2.2-1 所描繪的典型曲線呈下降趨勢 -- 隨著溫度上升，最大允許差壓逐步降低。務必查閱濾膜製造商的資格文件（Qualification Documentation），取得你所使用的特定濾膜型號在各溫度下的壓力限值。

            

**Leachables（可溶出物）的雙重風險：**

            

                
- 產品品質風險：溶出物可能與藥物活性成分交互作用

                
- 病患安全風險：某些溶出物可能有毒性

            

            

高溫操作時，Leachables 評估尤其重要，這與 Section 4（濾膜資格確認）中的 Extractables/Leachables 研究直接相關。

        

        

            

#### 圖表解讀 Figure Analysis

            

**Figure 5.2.2-1（溫度/壓力耐受性曲線）：**雖然此處無法顯示原圖，但典型的曲線樣態如下：

            

                
- X 軸 = 溫度（°C），從室溫到最高使用溫度

                
- Y 軸 = 最大允許差壓（bar 或 psi）

                
- 曲線向右下方傾斜：溫度越高，允許的最大壓力越低

                
- 通常在某個溫度點會有一個顯著的轉折點，超過該點後壓力限值急劇下降

            

            

**實務意義：**在進行製程設計時，必須在此曲線的安全區域內操作，並留有適當的安全餘量。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果你需要過濾一個必須在 60°C 操作的產品，你需要向濾膜供應商確認哪些資訊？

                
2. 溫度升高同時降低黏度（有利）和降低壓力耐受度（不利），你如何在實際操作中平衡這兩個因素？

                
3. 為什麼反向流動通常被視為壓力限值的最差情境？在什麼操作步驟中可能發生反向流動？

            

        

    

5.2.3 Filtration Time

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Filtration time (duration) is the amount of time required to filter a single batch (or campaign) of production fluid. The process duration will differ depending on if the process is a single bulk-sterilizing filtration operation or an intermittent in-line-filtration operation used to maintain the level in a break tank connected to dosing pumps during a sterile filling process. Increasing filtration times may increase the potential for bacterial penetration; therefore, the filter retentive performance should be validated to the maximum product/filter contact time for the process (see Section 6.8).

        

As part of the development of the process an assessment should be conducted to determine the longest potential product-contact time with the sterilizing filter. The worst-case process time should include maximum filling-process duration, including manufacturing interruption scenarios prior to and during filtration.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**兩種過濾模式的時間特性：**

            

                
- **單次批量過濾（Single Bulk Filtration）：**將整批藥液一次性過濾到無菌儲槽。過濾時間相對固定且較短。

                
- **間歇式線上過濾（Intermittent In-line Filtration）：**配合充填機的速度，持續地將藥液過濾到 Break Tank（緩衝槽），由充填泵取用。過濾時間等於整個充填製程的持續時間，可能長達數小時甚至整天。

            

            

**過濾時間 vs 產品接觸時間：**

            

                
- **過濾時間：**實際過濾的持續時間

                
- **產品接觸時間：**= 過濾時間 + 等待時間 + 中斷時間。這是更嚴格的定義，用於驗證。

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像你用濾水壺過濾自來水：

            

                
- **批量過濾：**一次倒滿一整壺水等它濾完 -- 接觸時間就是過濾完成所需的時間

                
- **線上過濾：**你邊喝水邊加水，濾水壺從早到晚一直在工作 -- 接觸時間是一整天

            

            

時間越長，細菌穿透濾膜的風險越高 -- 就像門開越久，蚊子飛進來的機會越大。所以驗證必須涵蓋最長的可能接觸時間。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Bacterial Penetration（細菌穿透）風險與時間的關係：**時間是細菌截留驗證中的關鍵最差情境參數。原因包括：

            

                
- 長時間接觸讓細菌有更多機會尋找並穿透膜孔

                
- 某些細菌在接觸濾膜後可能改變形態（如縮小體積）

                
- 長時間浸泡可能影響濾膜材料的完整性

            

            

**Manufacturing Interruption Scenarios（製造中斷情境）：**最差情境時間必須包含非計畫性中斷。例如：充填機故障、環境監測警報、設備清潔等可能導致過濾暫停但濾膜仍與產品接觸的情境。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 情境：**你的充填線通常一個批次充填 8 小時，但偶爾會遇到設備故障需要暫停 2 小時，且生產操作規範允許最多暫停兩次。那麼你的最差情境產品接觸時間 = 8 + 2 + 2 = 12 小時。你的細菌截留驗證必須涵蓋至少 12 小時的接觸時間，否則一旦實際生產超過驗證範圍，該批次可能面臨合規性質疑。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 在你的工廠中，除菌過濾的最大產品接觸時間是多少？是否已將所有可能的中斷情境納入考量？

                
2. 批量過濾和線上過濾的時間風險有何不同？哪種模式需要更嚴格的時間驗證？

            

        

    

5.3 Filter Throughput and Maximum Volume

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Filter throughput, or capacity, is the measurement of a total volume that can be filtered through the EFA under defined process conditions. Filter capacity depends on membrane material, porosity, pore size, nonspecific adsorption, pore shape, filtration area, pressure differential, contaminant load, and the physical properties of the product type being filtered. Table 5.3-1 lists potential factors affecting throughput.

        

Many process fluids that undergo sterilizing filtration are in the final formulation and do not result in significant fouling or filter-flux degradation over any practical volume. In many cases, there is no practical limit to the throughput, while in other cases, there can be particulate matter or subvisible particles present in the filtrate that do limit the filter throughput. In some cases, the prior processing history of the filtrate can affect the capacity (e.g., high-shear mixing of monoclonal antibodies can generate agglomerates) (27). Appropriate scale-down studies can be used to determine these behaviors as outlined in Section 5.4. Even in the case where no defined maximum filter capacity can be determined, the maximum volume that will be filtered should be specified so it can be covered during the filter-validation studies (see Section 6.8).

        

        
            Table 5.3-1 Factors Affecting Throughput
            
                
                
            
| Higher Total Throughput | Lower Total Throughput |
| --- | --- |
            
                
                
            
| High Porosity/Higher Void Volume | Low Porosity/Lesser Void Volume |
            
                
                
            
| Large Pore Size | Small Pore Size |
            
                
                
            
| Low Nonspecific Adsorption | High Nonspecific Adsorption |
            
                
                
            
| Asymmetric Pore Shape | Isotropic Pore Shape |
            
                
                
            
| High Effective Filtration Area (EFA) | Low Effective Filtration Area (EFA) |
            
                
                
            
| Low Contaminant Load | High Contaminant Load |
            
                
                
            
| Nondeformable, Hard Contaminant | Deformable, Soft Contaminant |
            
                
                
            
| Low Shear-Stress History | High Shear-Stress History |
        

        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Filter Throughput（濾膜通量/容量）：**在特定製程條件下，一支濾膜能處理的總體積。這與 Flow Rate（流速）不同 -- 流速是「多快」，通量是「多少」。

            

**Table 5.3-1 的關鍵洞見：**

            

                
- **Asymmetric vs Isotropic Pore Shape（非對稱 vs 等向孔形）：**非對稱膜的孔隙從進料側到出口側逐漸收窄，形成漸進式截留，能容納更多粒子 → 通量更高

                
- **Deformable, Soft Contaminant（可變形軟質污染物）：**軟質粒子（如蛋白質聚集體）會被壓入膜孔，堵塞更嚴重 → 通量更低。硬質粒子則停留在表面，不會深入堵塞

                
- **Shear-Stress History（剪切應力歷史）：**製程上游的高剪切操作（如高速攪拌）可能產生蛋白質聚集體，直接影響過濾通量

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像你在用咖啡濾紙沖咖啡：

            

                
- **流速（Flow Rate）：**水流過濾紙的速度 -- 「多快」

                
- **通量（Throughput）：**這張濾紙在堵塞之前總共能沖幾杯 -- 「多少」

                
- **軟質 vs 硬質污染物：**細咖啡渣（軟、可變形）會鑽進濾紙纖維裡，很快堵死。粗咖啡豆碎片（硬）停在表面，濾紙能用更久

                
- **前段製程影響：**如果你把咖啡豆磨得太細（= 高剪切），濾紙堵塞得更快

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**許多最終配方不會造成堵塞：**TR26 特別指出，很多經過除菌過濾的藥液是最終配方，實際上不會造成明顯的濾膜堵塞。在這些情境中，通量限制不是技術問題，但你仍然需要指定一個最大過濾體積用於驗證。

            

**高剪切攪拌的影響：**TR26 引用了一個重要案例 -- 單株抗體的高剪切攪拌會產生聚集體（agglomerates），直接影響過濾通量。這提醒我們：過濾性能不只取決於當下的操作條件，還受上游製程歷史的影響。

            

**即使沒有通量限制也要指定最大體積：**這是驗證要求。驗證必須有明確的邊界條件。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 情境：**你的客戶提供了一個 mAb 產品用於除菌過濾。在小規模測試中，你發現過濾到 500 L/m² 時流速開始明顯下降。進一步調查發現，客戶的上游製程使用了高速攪拌器進行混合，產生了蛋白質聚集體。

            

解決方案：(1) 建議客戶降低攪拌速度或改用低剪切混合 (2) 增加預過濾步驟去除聚集體 (3) 增加 EFA（使用更大的濾膜）以確保足夠通量 (4) 將上游攪拌條件納入製程設計空間。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼 Asymmetric Pore Shape 比 Isotropic Pore Shape 能提供更高的通量？請從結構角度說明。

                
2. 如果你的製程液體在實際操作中從未造成濾膜堵塞，你是否還需要進行通量測試？為什麼？

                
3. 上游製程的剪切歷史如何影響下游的除菌過濾性能？這對 CDMO 的跨部門協作有什麼啟示？

            

        

    

5.4 Scale-Down Systems and Testing

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

PD activities are generally done at the bench-scale using scale-down systems to minimize material quantities and allow for faster and more efficient experimentation. In order for the scale-down systems to be representative of the larger scales used in manufacturing the available systems and scaling considerations are discussed in this section.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Scale-Down Systems（縮小規模系統）：**在實驗台規模（Bench-scale）模擬大規模生產的過濾條件。核心目的是用少量材料獲得具代表性的製程數據，用於預測商業化規模的性能。

            

關鍵要求：縮小規模系統必須能「代表」（Representative）大規模製造的過濾行為。這意味著不能隨便縮小 -- 需要保持關鍵參數（如 flux、ΔP、溫度）的一致性。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

縮小規模測試就像建築師做的建築模型：你用 1:100 的比例模型測試結構強度和空氣流動。模型必須按比例精確縮小，而不是隨意做一個小房子。同樣地，過濾的 scale-down 系統必須按 EFA 比例縮小，同時維持相同的流速（flux）和壓力條件，否則測試結果無法放大到實際生產。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

Scale-down 系統的「代表性」是整個製程開發的基礎。如果小規模測試的結果不能準確預測大規模表現，所有後續的設計決策都會建立在不可靠的數據上。這就是為什麼本節要深入討論可用的系統類型和放大考量。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼製程開發（PD）活動要在小規模而非大規模進行？除了節省材料，還有哪些考量？

                
2. 如果小規模測試結果與大規模生產結果不一致，你會從哪些方面排查原因？

            

        

    

5.4.1 Small Scale Device Testing

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Filter-screening is generally performed using the process fluid in a constant flow or constant pressure experimental setup. Traditionally, 25mm or 47 mm discs or disc composites (Figure 5.4.1-1) installed in holders (Figure 5.4.1-2) were used for these screening studies. With modern filtration systems, however, most filter manufacturers have developed specialized encapsulated discs or small pleated capsules that better represent the flow dynamics of full-sized filters and allow closer estimates of scaling by EFA (see Figure 4.2-2). The screening tests can also be helpful to determine potential prefilter combinations to optimize the total throughput and reduce fouling, where required. For yield-sensitive applications, filtrate samples can be taken at frequent intervals to determine any nonspecific adsorption effects. Small-scale device tests may not always accurately predict the actual process in regard to flow-path dynamics and pleat-density parameters, however, and therefore may not scale up in a linear fashion, so care must be taken in the experimental design to ensure that any throughput or flux limitations are well understood.

        

Figure 5.4.1-1 Filter Disc / Figure 5.4.1-2 Filter Disc Holder  
(Figures not available in text extraction — refer to original TR26 document p30)

        

Most filterability tests are performed by keeping pressure constant and measuring the decline in flow rate as a function of filtered volume. The pressure set-point should mimic production pressure conditions. Nevertheless, there are some applications that should be evaluated using constant flow rate, such as the filtration of media. For constant-flow testing, the flow rate is controlled while the pressure gradually increases until a maximum pressure is reached. This mode of testing avoids compression of contaminants that may be captured on the membrane surface, leading to membrane fouling. Either constant-flow or constant-pressure filterability tests can be used to predict manufacturing-scale performance. Ideally, small-scale tests should be performed using flux and pressure conditions representative of the manufacturing-scale process or a representative worst-case scenario.

        

The main output of these small-scale filtration studies is to develop and understand the flow curves and evaluate filter flux at different pressure conditions, thus allowing selection of the optimal filter size and configuration to use in the at-scale process. If properly designed, the fouling propensity of the filter and process fluid combinations can also determine a maximum filter-throughput value. With this information under representative temperature and process conditions, the process can be scaled up using the ratio of EFA.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**濾膜篩選（Filter Screening）的演進：**

            

                
- **傳統方法：**使用 25mm 或 47mm 平面濾膜片（Disc）安裝在支架上進行測試

                
- **現代方法：**使用封裝式濾膜片或小型皺褶膠囊（Small Pleated Capsule），更能代表實際生產中全尺寸濾膜的流動動力學

            

            

**兩種測試模式：**

            

                
- **恆壓測試（Constant Pressure）：**固定壓力，測量流速隨過濾體積的衰減。適用於大多數應用。

                
- **恆流速測試（Constant Flow Rate）：**固定流速，測量壓力隨過濾體積的上升。適用於含污染物的流體（如培養基），因為恆壓操作可能壓縮膜面的污染物導致更嚴重的堵塞。

            

            

**線性放大的限制：**由於流路動力學（Flow-path Dynamics）和皺褶密度（Pleat Density）的差異，小規模結果不一定能線性放大。實驗設計必須充分理解這些限制。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

小規模測試就像試穿衣服。傳統的 47mm 濾膜片測試就像看尺寸表估算 -- 只能得到大概的尺寸感。而現代的小型皺褶膠囊測試就像在店裡實際試穿小碼衣服 -- 更能感受到實際穿著時的合身程度和舒適度。

            

但即使是實際試穿，也不能保證同款的加大碼穿起來完全一樣 -- 放大後的版型可能有微妙差異。同樣地，小規模過濾測試的結果在放大到生產規模時，也可能出現非線性的偏差。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**恆壓 vs 恆流速的選擇邏輯：**

            

                
- 恆壓測試更常見，也是多數廠商推薦的默認方法

                
- 但對於含有可壓縮污染物的流體（如培養基），恆壓會將污染物壓入膜孔，導致不具代表性的嚴重堵塞

                
- 恆流速測試避免了這個問題，因為壓力是逐漸上升的

            

            

**Prefilter Combinations（預過濾組合）：**小規模測試也可以用來評估預過濾器（Prefilter）的效果 -- 在除菌級濾膜前增加一個孔徑較大的預過濾器，去除大粒子，延長除菌級濾膜的壽命，降低整體成本。

            

**Yield-Sensitive Applications（對收率敏感的應用）：**對於高價值生物製劑，必須在過濾過程中頻繁取樣檢測產品濃度，確認吸附損失在可接受範圍內。

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Formula

            

**EFA 比例放大計算：**

            

```

放大倍數 = EFA_production / EFA_small-scale

例如：
  小規模測試：EFA = 3.5 cm² (47mm disc)
  生產規模需處理 500L，小規模可處理 50 mL

  所需放大倍數 = 500,000 mL / 50 mL = 10,000
  生產規模所需 EFA = 3.5 cm² × 10,000 = 35,000 cm² = 3.5 m²

注意：此計算假設線性放大，實際可能需要
加入安全係數（通常 1.2-2.0x）以補償
非線性效應和皺褶密度差異。
            
```

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 情境：**你需要為一個新的 mAb 產品選擇除菌濾膜。你手上有三個候選濾膜廠商的小型測試膠囊。

            

**建議的篩選流程：**

            

                
1. 使用相同的製程液體，在恆壓條件下（模擬生產壓力）測試三支濾膜

                
2. 繪製流速 vs 過濾體積曲線（Flow Curve）

                
3. 比較各濾膜的通量（L/m²）、堵塞傾向和吸附表現

                
4. 選出最佳候選者後，用 EFA 比例計算生產規模所需的濾膜尺寸

                
5. 加入 1.5-2.0x 安全係數以補償放大過程中的不確定性

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼現代的小型皺褶膠囊比傳統 47mm 平面濾膜片更能代表生產規模的性能？從流動動力學角度說明。

                
2. 在什麼情況下你會選擇恆流速測試而非恆壓測試？請結合你的實際製程經驗回答。

                
3. 如果小規模測試顯示濾膜在 200 L/m² 時堵塞，但你的生產需求是 180 L/m²，你認為安全餘量是否足夠？你會如何決策？

# Section 5.0 Part B: Filtration Process Design, Usage, and Handling Considerations (5.4.2 - 5.9)

    

過濾製程設計、使用與操作考量（下篇：放大、系統設計、生物負荷、沖洗、安裝與滅菌影響）

    

PDA Technical Report No. 26 (Revised 2025) — Sterilizing Filtration of Liquids | p31 - p39

5.4.2 Filtration Process-Scaling Considerations

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Scaling up filtration performance from a laboratory-scale filter unit to a production-scale system, which might contain multiple cartridges or units, poses several challenges to the filter user. Challenges include, but are not limited to:

        

            
- Product for filter trials might be in limited supply due to high production costs and limited production runs.

            
- Surrogate fluids might not be representative of the actual process fluid for certain behaviors like fouling or non-Newtonian flow dynamics.

            
- Small-scale filter studies may not represent the conditions under which filtration occurs in the manufacturing process.

            
- Laboratory-scale filter elements used for testing may not be directly predictive of large-scale filter capacity.

        

        

To overcome these challenges, filter users may elect to work with the filter manufacturer(s) to design small-scale studies that either closely approximate production systems or, alternatively, rely on appropriate safety factors to account for unknown variables and ensure successful filtration operations at scale.

        

Careful attention should be paid to ensuring that the material used for the scale-down studies is representative of the materials used for commercial production. In the production of proteins, there have been several documented examples where shear stresses imparted on the molecule upstream in the process result in the formation of subvisible particulates that can cause filter-fouling (27). In many cases the same solution that has not been subjected to the same levels of shear stress will show no signs of fouling behavior; this represents a scale-up risk that can be difficult to characterize that can manifest itself as filter-clogging during production. In this instance, considerable study may be required to create appropriate scale-down models of this shear behavior, as not all protein solutions and mixer types react in the same fashion. This is just one example of the importance of understanding the full-scale process and the stress history of the filtrate and how they affect filtration performance. There are also instances where freeze-thaw or shipping conditions of solutions, such as lipid nanoparticles (LNPs) or lentivirus drug products can affect the filtration performance (e.g., reduced volume throughput). It is critical that the impact of these factors is understood to ensure small-scale studies provide representative data.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Scale-Up（放大）vs Scale-Down（縮小模擬）：**過濾製程開發通常從實驗室小規模開始，再放大至生產規模。Scale-down study（縮小模擬研究）是用小型設備模擬生產條件，以最少的原料獲得最多的數據。

            

**Shear Stress（剪切應力）：**蛋白質溶液在上游製程中經過泵浦、攪拌、管路等設備時所受到的機械力。高剪切力可能導致蛋白質聚集形成次可見微粒（subvisible particulates），進而堵塞除菌濾膜。

            

**Surrogate Fluid（替代流體）：**當實際產品供應有限或成本過高時，使用模擬液替代實際產品進行初步測試。但替代液可能無法完全模擬真實產品的阻塞行為。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像你在自家廚房（實驗室）用小鍋試做一道菜的食譜，覺得很成功。但當你搬到婚宴廚房（生產規模）用大鍋煮同一道菜時，火候不均、攪拌力道不同、食材批次差異，結果可能完全不一樣。Scale-down study 就像是在大鍋的環境條件下，刻意用小鍋重新模擬，才能真正預測大鍋出菜的品質。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**蛋白質的「壓力歷史」極為重要：**同一批蛋白質溶液，在不同的上游製程設備（不同攪拌器、不同泵浦）處理後，可能展現完全不同的過濾行為。這就是為什麼 TR26 特別強調必須理解 filtrate 的 stress history（應力歷史）。

            

**LNP 和慢病毒產品的特殊風險：**冷凍解凍（freeze-thaw）或運輸條件可能改變這些新型藥物的物理特性，導致過濾通量大幅下降。在進行小規模研究時，必須使用經歷過相同處理歷程的物料。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 環境中，客戶常提供有限量的臨床批次物料進行製程開發。如果你只用 WFI 做過濾測試而跳過真實產品測試，到了 GMP 生產時才發現濾膜堵塞，代價極其高昂——不僅浪費一整批產品，還可能延誤臨床進度。建議做法：至少用一部分真實產品進行小規模過濾研究，搭配安全係數（safety factor，通常 1.5-2x）來補償未知變數。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼同一個蛋白質溶液在實驗室不會堵塞濾膜，但在工廠卻會堵塞？可能的原因有哪些？

                
2. 如果你的客戶只能提供 500 mL 的藥品進行過濾開發研究，你會如何設計試驗以最大化數據價值？

                
3. 為什麼 LNP 藥品的運輸條件會影響過濾性能？這對 CDMO 的物料接收程序有什麼影響？

            

        

    

5.5 Filtration System Design and Integration

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

A user requirement specification (URS) is a helpful tool in designing a SUS or stainless-steel setup. The filter user should have detailed knowledge of all process operational parameters to define the requirements of a particular assembly. The suitability of particular components depends on the requirements of the product and process. URSs typically include:

        

            
- Flow rate

            
- Pressure conditions

            
- Temperature conditions

            
- MoC

            
- Filter (pore size, area)

            
- Product volumes

            
- Instrumentation

            
- Sampling requirements

            
- System configuration

            
- Fluid properties

            
- Integrity-test methods and needs

            
- Sterilization method

            
- Documentation requirements

        

        

In addition to the integrity-test considerations stated in Section 7.0, the following points should be considered for filtration systems:

        

            
- Pressurization of the upstream side of the filter with gas after wetting

            
- Need for a downstream vent filter to accommodate the gas flow

            
- Mechanism to aseptically remove the wetting fluid from the system, if necessary

            
- Use of a hydrophilic drain filter and a separate hydrophobic vent filter or other appropriate valves and drains for the system

            
- Use of a combination hydrophilic/hydrophobic vent filter, where applicable

            
- Appropriate placement of process controls, such as pressure sensors or flowmeters, and required sampling locations

        

        

            "Note: Use of separate filters enables both to be integrity-tested in situ with water, whereas a combination hydrophilic/hydrophobic filter can only be tested with alcohol, off-line."
        

        

The qualification tests listed in Section 4.1 are performed within the manufacturer's defined conditions. Assemblies of components require validation within the filter/single-use user's process and environment. Validation should be performed to cover actual or worst-case process conditions, preferably with the product or a model (surrogate) solution. The single-use component or assembly should meet process and regulatory requirements. The validation effort should ensure that the components/assembly functions as intended and does not negatively influence product attributes, neither the product and process conditions, nor the single-use components or assembly.

        

Furthermore, functionality tests verify that desired process conditions, (e.g., filtration time) can be met. Documented evidence should be established that operational parameter specifications can be met repeatedly.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**User Requirement Specification / URS（使用者需求規格書）：**在設計過濾系統之前，必須先將所有製程參數、品質需求、法規要求以書面形式定義清楚。URS 是設計的起點，也是後續驗證的基準。

            

**Hydrophilic vs Hydrophobic Filter（親水性 vs 疏水性濾膜）：**親水性濾膜用於過濾液體（包括排水），疏水性濾膜用於過濾氣體（通氣）。在完整性測試的便利性上，選擇分開的濾膜 vs 組合式濾膜會有不同的測試策略影響。

            

**Worst-Case Process Conditions（最差條件）：**驗證必須涵蓋實際或最差的製程條件，這是確保商業生產過程中無論遇到什麼情況，過濾系統都能正常運作的關鍵原則。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

URS 就像是你蓋房子之前的建築需求書——要幾間房、多大的客廳、需要什麼管線、承重多少。沒有清楚的 URS 就開始組裝過濾系統，就像沒有藍圖就開始蓋房子：等發現管線不通或承重不足時，改建成本遠高於一開始就規劃好。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**分開式 vs 組合式濾膜的完整性測試差異：**這是一個容易被忽略但對實務影響很大的決策。如果使用組合式親水/疏水濾膜，就只能用酒精離線測試（off-line），這代表需要額外的操作步驟和風險。分開設置則可以在位（in situ）用水測試，操作更簡便也更符合法規期望。

            

**製造商資格確認 ≠ 使用者驗證：**濾膜製造商在其定義的條件下做的 qualification test，不能直接替代使用者在自己的製程環境中進行的 validation。CDMO 必須在自身的實際製程條件下證明系統可行。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 列出你設計一個新的除菌過濾系統時，URS 中最關鍵的五個參數，並說明為什麼它們最重要。

                
2. 在什麼情況下你會選擇組合式親水/疏水濾膜，而非分開設置？這個決策需要考慮哪些因素？

                
3. 為什麼濾膜製造商的 qualification data 不能直接取代使用者的 process validation？

            

        

    

5.5.1 Multiple Filters in Series

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Manufacturing processes are frequently designed with trains of multiple filters in a series (sequential flow through one filter after another), but the purpose of these extra filters varies from process to process, and the design and purpose of each filter must be clearly documented.

        

### 5.5.1.1 Two-Filter Sterilization (Double Filtration)

        

In uncommon processes, where two filters together in series are both required to achieve sterility and the train has been validated to achieve the sterilization of a specific product only when passing through both filters, the filter train can be considered a single sterilizing unit, and both filters must successfully pass the integrity test.

        

### 5.5.1.2 Pre-Filtration

        

One of the most common purposes for additional filters upstream of the final sterilizing filter is for prefiltration functions, as opposed to sterilization. An example is bioburden reduction that may be performed with a sterilizing-grade filter, but the filter is not performing a strict sterilizing function. Rather, it is assuring that a very low bioburden level is present before entering the final sterilizing filter.

        

Other prefilters may be performing functions unrelated to microbial control, such as aggregate or particle removal prior to the final sterilizing filtration, that may not use sterilizing-grade filters.

        

### 5.5.1.3 Redundant Filtration

        

Processes where an additional (redundant) sterilizing filter is placed in the filter train to ensure against loss of product due to potential-integrity test failure of the primary sterilizing filter. The additional "secondary" filter is typically identical to the primary sterilizing filter, is fully validated to sterilize the fluid on its own and undergoes post-use integrity-testing as a contingency in the event the primary filter fails. Generally, the filter closest to filling (farthest downstream) should be the primary filter (10). The pressure and flow-rate controls are generally designed to apply across both sterilizing filters.

        

Figure 5.5-1, Figure 5.5-2, Figure 5.5-3, and 5.5-4 illustrate different filter trains that can be used for the filtration operation (see Section 7.4.3 for additional information).

        

*Note: DP/DS stands for drug product/drug substance.*

        

*Figure 5.5-1 Single Filter Train Configuration*

        

*Figure 5.5-2 Pre-Filter Train Configuration*

        

*Figure 5.5-3 Redundant Sterilizing Filter Train Configuration*

        

*Figure 5.5-4 "Double" Filtration Train Configuration (uncommon)*

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**三種串聯過濾配置的區別：**

            

                
- **Double Filtration（雙重除菌過濾）：**兩支濾膜「共同」完成除菌功能，缺一不可，視為單一除菌單元。這是罕見的配置，通常只用於特殊產品。

                
- **Pre-Filtration（前過濾）：**上游濾膜負責降低生物負荷或去除微粒，保護下游的最終除菌濾膜，但本身不是執行「除菌」功能。

                
- **Redundant Filtration（冗餘過濾）：**備用除菌濾膜，各自獨立具備完整的除菌能力。當主濾膜完整性測試失敗時，備用濾膜可以保住整批產品。

            

            

**Primary Filter（主要濾膜）位置：**一般應將最靠近充填端（最下游）的濾膜定為主要濾膜。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像機場的安檢流程：

            

                
- **Pre-filtration** = 行李 X 光機（初步篩選，去除明顯的禁止物品）

                
- **Redundant filtration** = 雙重安全門——即使第一道門故障，第二道門仍然能完全攔截

                
- **Double filtration** = 一道安檢需要兩個設備同時運作才能完成檢測（非常罕見的特殊設計）

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Redundant filtration 的經濟學邏輯：**多加一支除菌濾膜的成本可能只有幾千美元，但如果主濾膜完整性測試失敗而沒有備用濾膜，整批產品（可能價值數十萬到數百萬美元）就必須報廢。這是一個非常清楚的風險管理決策。

            

**每支濾膜的目的必須明確文件化：**法規機構會審查每支濾膜在 filter train 中的角色定位。如果文件不清楚——例如 pre-filter 被描述為「除菌」功能——可能會引發額外的驗證要求。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 環境中，不同客戶的產品可能需要不同的 filter train 配置。建議建立標準的平台配置（例如：pre-filter + redundant sterilizing filter 作為基本配置），然後根據產品特性和客戶需求進行調整。這樣可以減少系統設計和驗證的重複工作，同時確保每個案子都有清楚的文件說明每支濾膜的功能定位。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果你的 redundant filter 和 primary filter 都通過了使用後完整性測試，是否還需要保留 redundant filter 的配置？為什麼？

                
2. 在什麼樣的產品特性下，你可能需要考慮 double filtration 而非 redundant filtration？

                
3. 為什麼 primary filter 通常設在最下游（最靠近充填）的位置？

            

        

    

5.6 Pre-Filtration Bioburden Monitoring

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

An important aspect of filtration process design is pre-filtration bioburden monitoring: a common regulatory expectation. The inlet to the final sterilizing filter should have well-controlled bioburden levels, despite the extreme bacterial removal efficiency typically validated in retention studies (see Section 6.6) (28). The difference between the low bioburden levels routinely entering the sterilizing filter, and the high levels validated to be removed by retention studies provides a large safety factor which is an important principle in sterilization by filtration. Factors to consider when designing a pre-filtration bioburden monitoring program include:

        

            
- Relevant regulatory expectations for allowable bioburden limit (i.e., the acceptance criteria of the test)

            
- Representative sampling time:
                

                    
    - If bioburden levels could rise over the course of the filtration operation, sampling at or near the end of the filtration could be warranted. For short filtration durations or bacteriostatic/bactericidal fluids, sampling at the beginning of the filtration may be appropriate.

                

            

            
- Location of the sample: the pre-filtration bioburden sample should be taken immediately upstream of the sterilizing filter (or, in cases of redundant filtration, upstream of the first sterilizing filter), and downstream of any bioburden reduction filters.

            
- Impact of preservatives on the bioburden assay.

        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Pre-Filtration Bioburden Monitoring（過濾前生物負荷監測）：**在液體進入最終除菌濾膜之前，測量其中的微生物含量。這是法規的普遍期望，目的是確認進入除菌濾膜的微生物負荷在可控範圍內。

            

**Safety Factor（安全係數）的概念：**細菌截留驗證研究（Section 6.6）通常使用極高的挑戰濃度（例如 107 CFU/cm2），而實際生產中進入濾膜的生物負荷遠低於此。這之間的差距就是安全係數——這個差距越大，無菌保證的信心越高。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

這就像機場安檢前的行李 X 光檢查。雖然安檢門（除菌濾膜）本身已經驗證過能攔截武器，但你仍然會希望在進入安檢門之前就先用 X 光掃描過行李，確認大部分問題物品已經被提前發現。這樣即使安檢門偶爾出現小失誤，整體安全仍然有保障。Pre-filtration bioburden monitoring 就是那個行李 X 光。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**取樣時間點的選擇至關重要：**

            

                
- 如果產品不含抑菌成分且過濾時間較長，微生物可能在過濾過程中增殖，此時應在過濾「結束時」取樣，代表最壞情況。

                
- 如果產品本身具有抑菌性（如含防腐劑），微生物不太可能在過濾過程中增長，可在過濾「開始時」取樣。

            

            

**取樣位置：**必須在除菌濾膜的「緊前方」取樣——如果有 bioburden reduction filter 在更上游，取樣點應在其下游但除菌濾膜上游。

            

**防腐劑對檢測的干擾：**某些防腐劑會抑制或殺死檢測培養中的微生物，導致假陰性結果。需要在方法學驗證中考慮此因素。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果你的產品含有 0.02% 多聚山梨酯 80（Polysorbate 80，非抑菌濃度），過濾時間為 4 小時，你會在什麼時間點取 bioburden 樣品？為什麼？

                
2. 為什麼即使細菌截留驗證已經證明濾膜能截留極高濃度的細菌，法規仍然要求監測 pre-filtration bioburden？

                
3. 如果 pre-filtration bioburden 超出了接受標準，你會採取什麼措施？這會影響批次放行嗎？

            

        

    

5.7 Flushing Conditions/Filter Priming

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Sterilizing-grade filters generally must be flushed and primed prior to use, either in the process of integrity-testing or as a separate step, and filter manufacturers typically have recommendations for minimum flush volumes. Pre-use flushing with water for injection (WFI), buffer, product, or sequential combinations as necessary may be used to reduce leachables and can be important to reduce the level of nonspecific adsorption and ensure that the filtrate is homogeneous during the process. Filter-priming is also necessary to remove air from the filters and ensure that the filter membrane is fully wet thus making use of all of the filter EFA during the process. For specific flushing considerations related to pre-use post-sterilization integrity test (PUPSIT) refer to Section 7.0.

        

Pre-use flush volumes are typically determined empirically at scale for each installation based on the needs of the process. Depending on the propensity of the filter to adsorb the product or excipients contained in the product stream, there may also be a specific flushing solution used. For example, polysorbate or poloxamer surfactants are common excipients in the final formulation of many protein-based pharmaceutical products. Depending on the filter chemistry and the formulation composition, the saturation of adsorption sites on the filter material with these excipients can occur considerably slower than the saturation of adsorption sites that chemically bind the protein active ingredient, leading to reduced excipient concentrations at the beginning of the filtration. In these instances, a surfactant containing flush buffer can considerably reduce the required product flush volume, significantly increasing the product yield.

        

The flush steps can be estimated using a scale down system, although due to the flow dynamics and different surface area-to-volume ratios between small-and-large scales, they require confirmation at full scale. In these instances, a larger flush volume, calculated as a multiple of the EFA-ratio scale-down volume required, is used, the flush is done in a stepwise fashion, and the material is collected after the filter. This fractionated material can then be subjected to characterization testing, such as TOC, excipient concentration, or protein-specific assays that can be used to generate a filter-flush curve to determine when the leachables are removed, the filter reaches saturation equilibrium and the filtrate is completely homogeneous. Nonproduct flushes may need to be chased with a product flush to avoid diluting effects and return the filtrate to a homogeneous state.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Filter Flushing（濾膜沖洗）：**使用 WFI、緩衝液或產品沖洗濾膜，目的有三：(1) 降低可溶出物（leachables）含量，(2) 飽和濾膜的吸附位點以減少非特異性吸附，(3) 確保濾液均質。

            

**Filter Priming（濾膜排氣潤濕）：**排除濾膜中的空氣，確保膜體完全潤濕，讓所有有效過濾面積（EFA）都參與過濾。未完全潤濕的區域等於浪費了付費購買的過濾面積。

            

**Filter-Flush Curve（濾膜沖洗曲線）：**透過分段收集沖洗液並進行分析（TOC、賦形劑濃度等），繪製出隨沖洗體積增加，leachables 下降和濾液均質化的曲線，用以確定最適沖洗量。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像泡茶。第一泡會釋出最多的雜味（類似 leachables），茶壺本身也會吸附一些茶的成分（類似非特異性吸附）。有經驗的泡茶師會先用熱水「潤壺」，然後倒掉第一泡，這樣正式泡出來的茶味道才純正均勻。Filter flushing 的道理完全一樣——先沖洗掉雜質、飽和吸附位點，後續的產品濾液才能品質穩定。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**界面活性劑吸附的時間差問題：**這是一個在蛋白質藥品製造中非常實際的問題。Polysorbate 80 等界面活性劑在濾膜上的吸附飽和速度可能比蛋白質活性成分慢得多，導致過濾初期的濾液中界面活性劑濃度不足。如果不處理這個問題，初期產品可能因為界面活性劑不足而不符合配方規格。

            

**解決方案：**使用含界面活性劑的緩衝液預先沖洗濾膜，先飽和吸附位點，這樣可以大幅減少需要丟棄的產品沖洗量，直接提升產品回收率。

            

**小規模 vs 全規模確認：**沖洗量可以用小規模試驗估算，但由於流體動力學差異和表面積/體積比的不同，最終必須在全規模下確認。

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Formula

            

```

沖洗量放大估算：
全規模沖洗量 = 小規模沖洗量 × (全規模 EFA / 小規模 EFA) × 安全係數

例：小規模 (EFA = 13 cm²) 需要 50 mL 沖洗
    全規模 (EFA = 13,000 cm²)：
    = 50 mL × (13,000/13) × 1.5
    = 50 mL × 1,000 × 1.5
    = 75,000 mL = 75 L

安全係數通常取 1.2-2.0，視應用而定
```

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

對於高價值的蛋白質藥品（例如單株抗體），每毫升產品可能價值數百美元。如果需要丟棄 5 L 的產品沖洗液，損失可能高達數十萬美元。透過開發含界面活性劑的預沖洗步驟，將產品沖洗量從 5 L 降至 1 L，每批次可節省大量成本。這類工藝優化在 CDMO 中是重要的附加價值服務。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼 polysorbate 在濾膜上的吸附飽和速度比蛋白質慢？這與兩者的分子特性有什麼關係？

                
2. 如何設計一個 filter-flush curve 實驗來確定最適沖洗量？你會測量哪些指標？

                
3. 為什麼非產品沖洗液之後還需要用產品再沖洗一次（product chase）？

            

        

    

5.8 Filter Handling and Installation

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

An important part of the development of a sterilizing filtration process involves the installation and handling of the sterilizing filters in the manufacturing environment. Filter cartridges must be installed into a filter housing. Filters encapsulated in a polymeric housing may be part of a pre-assembled SUS assembly. Most commonly, the filter cartridge will be installed into the filter housing and heat sterilized via in-line steam sterilization or autoclaving. Capsule filters are commonly supplied presterilized via irradiation, or they can be autoclaved by the end user.

        

### 5.8.1 Cartridge Handling and Installation Considerations

        

By following these guidelines for cartridge-handling during the development of the process, users can ensure the proper installation, maintenance, and performance of the filtration system.

        

**1. Identification and Receipt**

        

            
- Cartridges should be identified by checking the part number, lot number, and description.
