## Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Worst-Case Test Parameters (最差條件測試參數):** 在設計細菌截留驗證研究時，必須選擇能「涵蓋」實際製造條件的最差情境參數。這些參數不是隨意放大，而是基於製程開發 (PD) 階段確定的數據，加上合理且有依據的安全係數 (safety factor)。

            

**Time-Dependent Penetration (時間依賴性穿透):** 隨著過濾時間延長，細菌可能逐漸通過濾膜。這與濾膜相容性劣化、完整性維持能力下降等因素有關，因此挑戰試驗必須涵蓋完整的製程時間。

            

**Flux Scaling (通量縮放):** 實驗室規模的細菌截留研究需要將流量縮放為單位面積通量 (ml/min)/cm2，以確保與生產規模具有等效性。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

最差條件設計就像**防火演習時選擇最困難的撤離路線**：你不會只演練最簡單的出口，而是模擬煙霧最濃、距離最遠、人數最多的情境。如果在這種極端條件下都能安全撤離，日常情況自然沒問題。同樣地，如果濾膜在最高壓力、最長時間、最高黏度的組合下仍能完全截留細菌，正常製程條件就更有把握了。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Table 6.6.6-1 是實務設計的「檢查清單」：**

            

                
- **黏度 ↑** = 壓力 ↑ = 穿透風險 ↑

                
- **表面張力 ↓** = 脂質體等高風險流體更容易讓細菌穿過

                
- **滲透壓 ↑** = 細菌細胞可能縮小，更容易通過

                
- **pH 中性** = 最支持微生物生長，因此是最差條件

                
- **離子強度極端值** = 可能影響吸附截留 (Adsorptive Sequestration) 機制

            

            

特別注意溫度是「Case-specific」的三向考量：低溫增加黏度、室溫支持微生物生長、高溫可能暴露相容性問題。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Blowdown Simulation

            

Product recovery by blowdown（用氣壓將殘液吹出）往往使用比正常過濾更高的壓力。這個步驟必須在細菌截留研究的最後模擬，因為它代表了製程中濾膜承受的「最後一擊」。如果只測試正常過濾壓力而忽略 blowdown，就是漏掉了最差條件中的一個關鍵環節。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 實務情境：** 你的客戶有一個脂質體 (liposome) 製劑，要進行除菌過濾驗證。根據 Table 6.6.6-1，你需要特別關注：

            

                
- 表面張力較低 -- 脂質體本身就是高風險流體

                
- 產品可能含有脂質成分 -- 直接列為考量因素

                
- 溫度設定需三方考量

                
- Blowdown 壓力可能高於正常過濾壓力

            

            

身為 CDMO，你需要在驗證方案中逐項說明每個參數的最差條件選擇理由，這就是 QbD (Quality by Design) 思維在過濾驗證中的體現。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼 pH 中性被認為是最差條件，而不是極端酸鹼值？

                
2. 如果實驗室無法同時維持目標壓力和通量達到完整製程時間，有哪些替代方法可以納入研究設計？

                
3. 為什麼離子強度要考慮「極端值」而非單一方向（高或低）？這與哪種截留機制有關？

            

        

    

6.6.7 Factors to Consider for Bacterial Retention Study Design (incl. 6.6.7.1 – 6.6.7.5)

    

        

## Original Text

        

### 6.6.7 Factors to Consider for Bacterial Retention Study Design

        

If questions arise during protocol development regarding the acceptability of a testing methodology, it may be advisable to contact the appropriate regulatory agency for guidance. Figure 6.6.7-1 reflects key steps to be considered when selecting the appropriate validation strategy for a specific filter and product/process combination.

        

**Note: Concurrence of the appropriate regulatory agency should be sought prior to using this methodology.*

        

*Figure 6.6.7-1 Sterilizing Filtration Process Validation Strategy*

        

Irrespective of the test design used, it is important to include a 0.4/0.45 µm positive control filter in parallel with the test filters to assure organism size, monodispersion and viability. Other modifications for the 0.45 µm control filter may be appropriate if fully justified and still demonstrate the challenge organism is fit for purpose.

        

### 6.6.7.1 Non-bactericidal Processes and Fluids

        

Direct inoculation of the product with the challenge microorganism is the preferred method of validating microbial retention of a sterilizing-grade filter. This is possible with products and process fluids that have demonstrated no bactericidal effects from the product or processing conditions. For these processes, the product should be directly inoculated with the challenge organism at sufficient concentration and under simulated processing conditions, including time, pressure, flow rate, volume throughput and other critical variables (e.g., temperature) as indicated in Table 6.6.6-1. Dilution from bacterial inoculation should be minimized to prevent altering the product any more than necessary.

        

### 6.6.7.2 Bacteriostatic/Bactericidal/Nondispersive Challenge Fluids

        

Performing bacterial retention studies on bactericidal products makes it more difficult to answer questions relating to validation, such as What effect does the product have on the filter and what effect does the product have on flora within the product? Bacterial retention studies performed on a bactericidal formulation, or under challenge conditions adverse to microbial viability (e.g., elevated temperature), may not produce valid results.

        

To evaluate the potential effect of the product/process on the filter, the filter may be preconditioned with the product under simulated processing conditions, including flow rate, pressure, temperature, volume throughput and time. This preconditioning may be performed by recirculating the product through the test filter in a closed-loop system or by a single pass (which could include a static soak to meet required contact time) through the test filter, followed by the bacterial challenge. Section 6.6.7.3, Section 6.6.7.4, and Section 6.6.7.5 discuss examples of test-method modifications that may be used to accommodate this type of bacterial retention study. Other modification methods may be equally appropriate, however, if justified.

        

### 6.6.7.3 Reduced Exposure Time

        

In some instances, the challenge organism may not survive in the product for the total processing time. The product should be inoculated directly with the challenge organism at sufficient concentration near the end of the preconditioning phase of the challenge (see Figure 6.6.7-1). The duration of the bacterial retention study should be supported by the viability data.

        

An alternative is to expose the challenge microorganisms in the challenge fluid under static conditions. After exposing the challenge bacteria in the product at process temperature and preconditioning the filter by recirculating the product (without the bacteria) under simulated processing conditions, the filter could be challenged under worst-case processing conditions (e.g., differential pressure and flow rate). The challenge duration should be minimized to ensure the challenge microorganisms remain viable during the actual exposure, challenge, and recovery periods.

        

### 6.6.7.4 Modify Test Method Parameters

        

Test-method parameter modification is useful for challenging bactericidal products, since it can involve changing only one process variable, such as temperature. Using this approach maintains the product/challenge organism interaction. This approach does not account for all possible process/product interactions but should allow the use of the standard challenge organism. After preconditioning the filter with the product under actual process conditions, the bactericidal component of the process (e.g., temperature) is modified and the bacterial retention study performed. The product should be inoculated directly with the bacterial retention study microorganism at a sufficient concentration (see Figure 6.6.7-1).

        

### 6.6.7.5 Modifying Test Product Formulation

        

Another modified method is to remove the bactericidal component from the product for the bacterial retention study following preconditioning of the filter with the actual product. This may be as simple as adjusting the pH to a nonbactericidal range, removing or diluting the bactericidal component, or using a surrogate fluid. Whatever approach is used should be supported by a technical rationale.

        

The modified formulation should be inoculated directly with the challenge organism at a sufficient concentration under simulated product processing conditions (see Figure 6.6.7-1). The bactericidal agent should be removed to a level that eliminates its interference with the challenge microorganism.

        

Another option is to precondition the test and control filters with the bactericidal process fluid under simulated worst-case processing conditions. After removing the bactericidal fluid from the test rig, the filters can then be challenged with the test organism suspended in surrogate fluid that has been justified to resemble the process fluid (e.g., chemical or physical properties). Other test modifications may also be acceptable if justified.

    

    

        

## Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Positive Control Filter (正對照濾膜，0.45 µm):** 在每次細菌截留研究中，必須與測試濾膜並行使用 0.45 µm 對照濾膜。這不是為了測試截留能力，而是為了確認挑戰菌株的大小、分散性和活性符合要求。如果對照濾膜無法回收細菌，就無法確認測試結果的有效性。

            

**Direct Inoculation (直接接種法):** 最理想的方法 -- 直接將挑戰微生物加入產品中，在模擬製程條件下進行過濾。這種方法最能反映真實情境，但前提是產品本身不會殺死或抑制挑戰微生物。

            

**Preconditioning (預處理/預調理):** 當產品具有殺菌性時，先用實際產品在模擬條件下處理濾膜，讓濾膜「暴露」於產品對其可能產生的影響，再進行細菌挑戰。這樣分開兩步的設計，既評估了產品對濾膜的影響，又確保挑戰微生物的活性。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

細菌截留研究的三種策略就像**教練針對不同場地設計測試**：

            

                
- **6.6.7.1 直接接種法** = 在標準球場上直接比賽（產品不殺菌，條件最理想）

                
- **6.6.7.2 殺菌產品的預處理法** = 球場上有刺激性物質，所以先讓球員在場地上適應，再開始比賽

                
- **6.6.7.3-5 修改方法** = 因為場地太危險，所以要麼縮短比賽時間、改變一個場地條件、或者用類似但安全的場地進行測試

            

            

無論用哪種方法，都要有「裁判」（正對照濾膜）確認比賽規則有效。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 殺菌產品的三種修改策略

            

當產品會殺死挑戰微生物時，TR26 提供了三種漸進式的修改策略：

            

                
- **6.6.7.3 縮短暴露時間：**在預處理階段結束前才加入細菌，縮短細菌與殺菌產品的接觸時間。需要活性數據支持所選的時間長度。

                
- **6.6.7.4 修改測試方法參數：**只改變一個製程變數（如溫度），維持產品/微生物的交互作用。例如產品在 60°C 有殺菌性，則預處理後降至 25°C 再做挑戰。

                
- **6.6.7.5 修改產品配方：**移除殺菌成分（如調整 pH、稀釋殺菌劑）或使用替代流體 (Surrogate Fluid)。必須有技術理由支持修改的合理性。

            

            

這三種方法的共同前提是：濾膜必須先用實際產品在實際條件下預處理。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 法規溝通

            

TR26 特別提到：如果在方案開發過程中對測試方法的可接受性有疑問，**建議聯繫適當的法規機構**尋求指導。這在使用修改方法（6.6.7.3-5）時尤其重要，因為這些方法偏離了「直接接種」的金標準，需要充分的科學論證。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 決策樹：**收到客戶的新產品進行除菌過濾驗證時，第一步就是做 Bactericidal/Bacteriostatic 測試：

            

                
- **結果：不殺菌** → 直接走 6.6.7.1，用直接接種法，最簡單明確

                
- **結果：殺菌** → 評估殺菌速度和機制，選擇 6.6.7.3（縮短時間）、6.6.7.4（改條件）或 6.6.7.5（改配方）

                
- **不確定** → 先與法規機構溝通，確認方法可接受性

            

            

選擇哪種修改方法取決於產品的殺菌機制和嚴重程度。通常優先嘗試改最少變數的方法（6.6.7.3 > 6.6.7.4 > 6.6.7.5）。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼正對照濾膜（0.45 µm）在每次細菌截留研究中都是必要的？如果正對照沒有回收到細菌，試驗結果還有效嗎？

                
2. 一個含有 0.1% 苯酚作為防腐劑的注射液產品，你會選擇哪種修改策略？為什麼？

                
3. 比較 6.6.7.4（修改參數）和 6.6.7.5（修改配方）：哪一種保留了更多原始產品/濾膜交互作用的資訊？

            

        

    

6.6.8 Filtrate Sampling

    

        

## Original Text

        

Analysis of the entire challenge effluent is necessary to determine the ability of a sterilizing-grade filter to retain the bacterial challenge. This can be done either by direct passage through an appropriate analytical membrane installed downstream of the test filter (whereby any penetrating bacteria would be captured on the analytical membrane) or by filtrate collection in a sterile vessel and subsequent filtration through analytical membrane(s). The analytical membranes should have been qualified as fit for purpose and will usually have a maximum rating of 0.4 µm or 0.45 µm. Selection of the size and porosity should be based on the application conditions and should not prevent achieving the desired differential pressure across the test filter. Sampling a portion of the filtrate is insufficient to validate sterilizing filtration, because a small number of cells may have penetrated the filter and remain undetected in the portion of the filtrate not sampled and analyzed.

    

    

        

## Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Entire Effluent Analysis (全量濾液分析):** 細菌截留驗證要求分析**全部**的挑戰濾液，不允許只取部分樣品。這是因為即使只有極少數細菌穿透濾膜，部分取樣可能完全錯過這些穿透菌，導致假陰性結果。

            

**Analytical Membrane (分析膜):** 安裝在測試濾膜下游的 0.4/0.45 µm 膜，用於捕獲任何穿透測試濾膜的細菌。可以直接串聯安裝，也可以先收集濾液再過濾分析。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

這就像**機場安檢的行李全檢 vs 抽檢**：如果機場只 X 光掃描 10% 的行李（部分取樣），那 90% 未檢查的行李中可能藏著危險物品。除菌過濾驗證的邏輯完全一樣 -- 你必須「掃描」100% 的濾液，因為即使只有 1 個細菌穿透，也代表濾膜驗證失敗。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**「部分取樣不足以驗證除菌過濾」** -- 這是 TR26 的明確聲明。在實務中，有兩種全量分析方式：

            

                
- **線上法 (In-line):** 分析膜直接串聯在測試濾膜下游，濾液直接通過分析膜 -- 簡單直接

                
- **離線法 (Off-line):** 先將濾液收集到無菌容器中，再通過分析膜 -- 適合大量濾液或需要特殊處理的情況

            

            

注意分析膜的選擇不能影響測試濾膜的跨膜壓差，否則會改變測試條件。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果分析膜的孔徑選擇不當（例如太小），可能對測試結果產生什麼影響？

                
2. 為什麼 TR26 強調「分析膜應不影響測試濾膜的跨膜壓差」？這與 worst-case 設計有什麼關係？

            

        

    

6.6.9 Results Interpretation

    

        

## Original Text

        

Acceptance criteria for sterilizing-grade filter performance are met when no passage of the bacterial challenge is detected in three test filters with a valid positive control (i.e., bacterial recovery through the 0.45 µm-rated control filter). If passage is detected in one filter, and no assignable cause can be determined, retesting may be conducted (e.g., three filters from the failed membrane lot) following an investigation and risk assessment to determine a potential root cause. If bacterial penetration occurs in any of the triplicate tests, then the filter cannot be considered validated under the specified conditions. If an assignable cause for the failure can be determined (e.g., damage to the filter or breach in aseptic technique), the suspect lot of filters should also be retested for confirmation of the proposed root cause for the initial failure. If the filter fouls prior to achieving the target volume throughput, the bacterial retention study should be terminated and the resultant total challenge determined. An investigation into the cause of fouling should be performed and documented, and a new bacterial retention study design should be proposed to ensure volume throughput is met based on filterability test results.

    

    

        

## Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Acceptance Criteria (接受標準):** 三支測試濾膜全部零穿透 + 正對照有效回收 = 通過。這是「全有或全無」的標準，沒有「允許少量穿透」的灰色地帶。

            

**Assignable Cause (可歸因原因):** 當一支濾膜出現穿透時，需要調查是否有明確的外部原因（如濾膜損壞、無菌操作失誤）。有可歸因原因 vs 無可歸因原因，走的是不同的後續路徑。

            

**Filter Fouling (濾膜堵塞):** 如果濾膜在達到目標體積通量前就堵塞了，研究必須終止。這不代表「通過」，而是需要重新設計研究方案。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

結果判讀就像**考駕照的路考**：

            

                
- **三人同時考試**（三支濾膜），全部通過才算這個型號合格

                
- 如果一人犯規（一支穿透），要調查是**考場問題**（可歸因原因，如車輛故障）還是**能力不足**（無可歸因原因）

                
- 如果是考場問題，可以換一批考生重考；如果能力不足，代表這個駕訓班的教學方法（驗證條件）需要重新檢討

                
- 如果車子在考試中途拋錨（濾膜堵塞），考試無效，必須查明原因後重新安排

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**結果判讀決策樹：**

            

                
- **3/3 通過 + 正對照有效** → 驗證成功

                
- **1/3 失敗 + 有可歸因原因** → 調查 → 用該批次重測 3 支確認根本原因

                
- **1/3 失敗 + 無可歸因原因** → 調查 + 風險評估 → 可重測（如用失敗批次的 3 支濾膜）

                
- **重測任何一支仍失敗** → 該濾膜在該條件下無法被驗證

                
- **濾膜堵塞** → 調查堵塞原因 → 基於可過濾性測試重新設計方案

            

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Triplicate Testing Logic

            

```

驗證測試要求：
  測試濾膜數量：  3 支（triplicate）
  正對照濾膜：    0.45 μm × 1 支（並行測試）

判定邏輯：
  穿透 = 0 / 3 支  →  PASS（驗證通過）
  穿透 = 1 / 3 支  →  INVESTIGATE → 可能 RETEST
  穿透 ≥ 2 / 3 支  →  FAIL（該條件下驗證失敗）
  堵塞（未達目標體積）→  VOID → 重新設計
            
```

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼要求使用三支測試濾膜（triplicate）而非單支？這與統計信心有什麼關係？

                
2. 如果正對照濾膜（0.45 µm）也沒有回收到細菌，整個試驗的結果應如何判定？

                
3. 濾膜堵塞為什麼不能直接判定為「通過」（既然沒有細菌穿透）？

            

        

    

6.7 Considerations for Sterilizing-Grade Filters Configured in Series

    

        

## Original Text

        

When two final sterilizing-grade filters are configured in series, it is necessary to clarify whether the setup is redundant filtration or double filtration, sometimes referred to as additive filtration (see Section 5.5.1 for detailed descriptions of various filter train designs). When redundant filtration is used (i.e., only one filter is required to meet sterility and only one filter must meet post-use integrity-test specifications), the process-specific bacterial retention study should be based on only one filter. Double filtration means both filters are required to achieve sterility (usually determined from process-specific bacterial retention study), and both filters must therefore meet post-use integrity test specifications.

        

Regardless of whether the setup is redundant filtration or double filtration, extractables should be considered for both filters.

    

    

        

## Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Redundant Filtration (冗餘過濾):** 兩支濾膜串聯，但任何一支單獨就能達到無菌要求。第二支是「備份」，就像飛機有兩個引擎但一個就能飛。只需要一支通過使用後完整性測試。

            

**Double Filtration / Additive Filtration (雙重過濾 / 加成過濾):** 兩支濾膜串聯，兩支都是必要的才能達到無菌。兩支都必須通過使用後完整性測試。這通常發生在單支濾膜的細菌截留研究無法達到零穿透的情況。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像**雙重安全帶**的概念：

            

                
- **Redundant Filtration** = 安全帶 + 安全氣囊：安全帶本身就夠了，安全氣囊是額外保障。你只需要確認安全帶功能正常。

                
- **Double Filtration** = 兩道安全帶（因為一道不夠強）：兩道都必須檢查確認功能正常，缺一不可。

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**關鍵區別對驗證的影響：**

            

                
- **Redundant：**細菌截留研究基於單支濾膜；使用後完整性測試只需一支通過

                
- **Double：**細菌截留研究可能顯示單支不足；使用後完整性測試兩支都必須通過

                
- **共同點：**無論哪種，兩支濾膜的 Extractables (可萃取物) 都必須評估 -- 因為藥液會接觸到兩支濾膜

            

            

在決策層級中，這直接關聯到**無菌濾液保證 (Sterile Filtrate Assurance)** -- 如果不清楚是 redundant 還是 double，就無法正確設計驗證方案和完整性測試策略。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 情境：**客戶要求在無菌充填線上使用兩支 0.2 µm 串聯濾膜。你必須先確認：

            

                
- 這是 redundant 還是 double？查看細菌截留驗證數據。

                
- 如果是 redundant：每批只需測一支的使用後完整性，但 E&L 需評估兩支。

                
- 如果是 double：每批兩支都要測使用後完整性，且兩支都要通過。失敗任一支 = 批次面臨風險。

            

            

這個定義直接影響批次放行決策，務必在驗證方案中清楚定義。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼即使是 redundant filtration，extractables 仍然需要考慮兩支濾膜？

                
2. 如果你的 double filtration 中第二支濾膜使用後完整性測試失敗，該批次的處置方式與 redundant filtration 有何不同？

            

        

    

6.8 Chemical Compatibility of Filter

    

        

## Original Text

        

While compatibility of the filter is assessed during initial filter-selection by the end user, compatibility testing may also be performed as part of the final sterilizing-grade filter validation testing. Chemical compatibility testing should encompass the entire device and depends on the fluid, filtration temperature and contact time.

        

A summary of worst-case conditions for conducting compatibility testing is shown in Table 6.8-1.

        

### Table 6.8-1 Worst-Case Considerations for Compatibility Testing

        
            
                
                
                
            
| Description | Worst-Case | Rationale |
| --- | --- | --- |
            
                
                
                
            
| Temperature | Higher | Higher temperatures increase potential for chemical reactions |
            
                
                
                
            
| Duration | Higher | Longer durations may increase potential for chemical reactions |
            
                
                
                
            
| Properties of drug product | Consider pH extremes, solvent and product components | Based on risk assessment |
            
                
                
                
            
| Sterilization | Maximum sterilization conditions (e.g., maximum temperature, number of cycles) | Worst-case sterilization conditions may impart more stress on the filter |
        

        

An assessment of chemical compatibility could include bacterial retention study data, post-exposure integrity-testing, tensile strength, nonvolatile residue (NVR), extractables, particulates, flow rate, optical or scanning electron microscopy (SEM), burst pressure, and membrane/O-ring thickness (23).

    

    

        

## Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Chemical Compatibility (化學相容性):** 評估濾膜及其整個裝置（包含外殼、O-ring、支撐結構）在接觸藥液和經歷滅菌條件後，是否仍維持結構完整性和功能性。這不僅是膜材本身的問題，而是整個過濾裝置的問題。

            

**NVR (Nonvolatile Residue, 非揮發性殘留物):** 將濾膜浸泡液蒸發後剩餘的固體物質，是化學相容性評估的指標之一。NVR 增加可能暗示濾膜材料在溶解或降解。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

化學相容性測試就像**泡茶時茶壺的材質選擇**：紫砂壺泡普洱茶沒問題，但用來泡高酸性的水果茶可能會溶出有害物質。同樣地，一支濾膜與 pH 7 的緩衝液完美相容，但接觸 pH 2 的酸性溶液可能會導致材料降解。你必須用最具挑戰性的條件（最高溫、最長時間、最極端 pH）來測試，確保「茶壺」在任何「茶」的條件下都安全。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**化學相容性評估的完整工具箱：**

            

                
- **功能性指標：**細菌截留數據、暴露後完整性測試、流量變化

                
- **物理性指標：**抗張強度、爆破壓力、膜厚/O-ring 厚度

                
- **化學性指標：**NVR、可萃取物、微粒

                
- **顯微鏡觀察：**光學或 SEM（掃描電子顯微鏡）檢查膜結構變化

            

            

注意 Table 6.8-1 中滅菌條件也是最差條件之一 -- 濾膜先經歷最大次數的滅菌循環，再接觸最具挑戰性的藥液，這代表了累積壓力的最差情境。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼化學相容性測試必須涵蓋「整個裝置」而非只有濾膜本身？想想 O-ring 和外殼材質可能帶來什麼風險。

                
2. Table 6.8-1 中的四個最差條件因素，哪一個最容易在實務中被忽略？為什麼？

                
3. 如果暴露後完整性測試通過但 SEM 顯示膜表面有明顯變化，你會如何判定相容性？

            

        

    

6.9 Revalidation Considerations

    

        

## Original Text

        

Once a filter is validated for use in a given application, further validation may be required if changes to the filter or manufacturing process are made. Some changes that may require revalidation include, but are not limited to:

        

            
- Change in membrane type or filter materials of construction.

            
- Increase in process parameters (e.g., volume to be filtered through a given filter area, flux, pressure, duration)

            
- Change in filter configuration (e.g., cartridge to encapsulated device). While the process-specific bacterial retention study data will likely not be impacted, consideration should be given to a reassessment of extractables/leachables and compatibility.

            
- Product formulation changes (e.g., change in product concentration, pH)

            
- Change in sterilization method (revalidation of the extractables/leachables assessment and filter-integrity post-sterilization should be considered based on risk assessment with appropriate justification)

            
- Temperature of filtration.

            
- Use of a filter with the same membrane type but not from the same supplier.

        

        

A well-structured risk assessment should be performed by process and filtration experts to evaluate the potential impact of these changes. In line with internal policy for filter management, the filter end user should approve all changes that potentially impact the current good manufacturing processes (GMP) compliance of the system.

    

    

        

## Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Revalidation (再驗證):** 當已驗證的過濾製程發生變更時，需要評估是否需要重新進行部分或全部驗證測試。這不是「自動全部重做」，而是基於風險評估，判斷哪些驗證要素受到影響。

            

**Same Membrane, Different Supplier (同膜不同供應商):** 這是容易被忽略但非常重要的觸發條件。即使膜材規格相同，不同供應商的製造條件、品質控制可能不同，因此需要重新驗證。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

再驗證的邏輯就像**汽車保固條款**：你買了一台車並通過了安全檢驗（初始驗證），但如果你改裝了引擎（膜材變更）、換了更大的輪胎（製程參數增加）、把手排改成自排（配置變更）、換了不同品牌的零件（同膜不同供應商），保固可能失效 -- 你需要重新送檢確認改裝後的車輛仍然安全。

            

關鍵是：不是所有改裝都需要全面重檢。換個車內芳香劑（微小變更）不需要，但換引擎（重大變更）一定需要。這就是風險評估的價值。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**變更類型 vs 再驗證範圍對照：**

            

                
- **膜材/材料變更** → 可能需要全面再驗證（細菌截留 + E&L + 相容性 + 完整性）

                
- **製程參數增加** → 主要影響細菌截留驗證（需重新評估最差條件）

                
- **配置變更（如匣式改為封裝式）** → 細菌截留可能不受影響，但 E&L 和相容性需重新評估

                
- **配方變更** → 可能影響細菌截留、化學相容性和 E&L

                
- **滅菌方法變更** → 主要影響 E&L 和滅菌後完整性

                
- **同膜不同供應商** → 需要評估所有驗證要素，可能需要全面再驗證

            

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 變更控制情境：**供應商通知你，原來使用的 PES 膜濾芯將停產，建議更換為「等效」產品。你應該：

            

                
1. 啟動變更控制程序

                
2. 評估新濾芯與原濾芯的差異（膜材、外殼材料、結構設計）

                
3. 進行風險評估：是「同膜同供應商不同型號」還是「不同供應商的同膜材」？

                
4. 制定再驗證方案：至少需要 E&L 重新評估和化學相容性確認，可能需要重新進行細菌截留研究

                
5. 確保所有受影響產品的技術文件都更新

            

            

身為 CDMO，你可能同時服務多個客戶的產品，一個濾芯供應商變更可能觸發多個產品的再驗證 -- 這是營運規劃中必須考量的影響範圍。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼 TR26 特別提到「同膜不同供應商」需要再驗證？膜材規格相同不代表什麼？

                
2. 如果製程參數的變更是「降低」而非「增加」（例如降低壓力），是否仍需要再驗證？為什麼？

                
3. 在 CDMO 環境中，客戶發起的配方變更 vs 供應商發起的濾膜變更，各自的再驗證責任歸屬如何？

            

        

    

6.10 Miscellaneous

    

        

## Original Text

        

With the introduction of newer manufacturing modalities, such as advanced therapy medicinal products (ATMPs), additional factors may need to be considered for the purposes of filter validation. For example, small batch sizes, short shelf life, and physical properties (e.g., shear sensitivity) may require careful planning and potentially modified test procedures to achieve the goals of filter validation while meeting regulatory expectations.

    

    

        

## Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**ATMPs (Advanced Therapy Medicinal Products, 先進治療藥品):** 包括基因治療、細胞治療、組織工程等新型態藥品。這些產品的特性（小批量、短效期、剪切力敏感）對傳統的過濾驗證方法提出了新挑戰。

            

**Shear Sensitivity (剪切力敏感性):** 某些生物製品（如細胞治療產品）在過濾過程中可能因剪切力而受損，這增加了濾膜選擇和驗證設計的複雜性。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

傳統藥品的過濾驗證就像**測試標準尺寸的包裹能否安全通過郵局分揀系統**。但 ATMPs 是像**活體動物運送** -- 包裹（產品）本身有生命，怕擠壓（剪切力敏感）、不能久放（短效期）、每次只運少量（小批量）。你不能用同樣的標準分揀速度和壓力來處理它，需要全新的操作規範。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

6.10 雖然篇幅短，但釋放了重要訊號：**TR26 的原則適用於所有除菌過濾，但具體方法需要隨產品類型調整**。對 CDMO 而言，如果你的業務發展方向包含細胞/基因治療產品，過濾驗證能力的建設必須提前規劃，因為：

            

                
- 小批量意味著實驗室縮放比更小，可能需要特殊的小面積測試裝置

                
- 短效期意味著驗證時間表必須與生產時間表緊密協調

                
- 剪切力敏感性可能限制了可用的過濾壓力和流量範圍

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 對一個剪切力敏感的細胞治療產品，Table 6.6.6-1 中的哪些最差條件參數需要重新定義？

                
2. 小批量產品的過濾驗證中，「全量濾液分析」（6.6.8）的執行會比大批量更容易還是更難？為什麼？

            

        

    

    

### Section 6.0 完整重點回顧 Complete Section Summary

    

**Section 6.0 Product & Process-Specific Validation Testing（產品與製程專屬驗證測試）**是 TR26 的核心章節，涵蓋了除菌過濾驗證的全部要素。以下是整個 Section 6.0 的系統性回顧：

    

        
1. **驗證測試的目的與 QbD 思維 (6.1-6.2):** 除菌過濾驗證不是單純的「通過/不通過」測試，而是基於品質源於設計 (Quality by Design) 的系統性方法。驗證必須證明在最差條件下，特定濾膜與特定產品/製程的組合能可靠地達成無菌保證。

        
2. **吸附性考量 (6.3):** 濾膜可能吸附藥品中的有效成分或配方組分，影響產品品質。吸附評估是驗證不可或缺的一環，特別是對於低劑量或高價值生物製品。

        
3. **可萃取物與可溶出物 (Extractables & Leachables, 6.4):** 濾膜及其組件在製程條件下可能釋出化學物質到藥液中。E&L 評估遵循「E 為 L 的最差條件預測」原則，需要在製程條件下進行系統性研究，並與毒理學評估結合。

        
4. **細菌截留驗證 (Bacterial Retention, 6.5-6.6):** 整個驗證的核心 -- 證明濾膜能在模擬最差條件下完全截留挑戰微生物 (*Brevundimonas diminuta*, 短小單胞菌)。關鍵要素包括：
            

                
    - ASTM F838 作為基礎方法論（濾膜的「駕照考試」）

                
    - 必須使用三支測試濾膜 (triplicate) + 0.45 µm 正對照

                
    - 最差條件選擇必須基於 Table 6.6.6-1 的系統性評估

                
    - 殺菌產品需使用修改方法（縮短時間 / 改參數 / 改配方）

                
    - 全量濾液分析，不允許部分取樣

                
    - 結果判讀遵循嚴格的決策樹

            

        

        
5. **串聯濾膜 (Series Filters, 6.7):** 必須明確區分冗餘過濾 (redundant) 與雙重過濾 (double)，這直接影響驗證範圍和使用後完整性測試策略。無論哪種配置，E&L 都需要兩支濾膜共同評估。

        
6. **化學相容性 (Chemical Compatibility, 6.8):** 評估整個過濾裝置（不僅是濾膜）在接觸藥液和滅菌條件後的完整性。最差條件包括最高溫度、最長時間、最極端 pH 和最大滅菌次數的組合。

        
7. **再驗證 (Revalidation, 6.9):** 任何對濾膜、製程參數、產品配方或滅菌方法的變更都需要透過風險評估決定再驗證範圍。特別注意「同膜不同供應商」也是觸發條件。

        
8. **新型態藥品 (ATMPs, 6.10):** 細胞/基因治療等先進療法藥品的小批量、短效期、剪切力敏感性對傳統驗證方法提出新挑戰，需要創新的驗證策略。

    

    

**決策層級提醒：**在整個 Section 6.0 中，所有驗證決策始終遵循 TR26 決策層級 -- (1) 無菌濾液保證 (Sterile Filtrate Assurance) 永遠是最高優先級，(2) 產品品質/CQAs 保護患者安全，(3) 製程穩健性確保可靠運營，(4) 商業與效率只在前三者都滿足後才考量。驗證測試的根本目的，就是為這個決策層級提供科學證據基礎。

## Section 7: Integrity Testing 完整性測試 (p56-p70)

# Section 7.0 Integrity Testing

    

完整性測試

    

PDA Technical Report No. 26 (Revised 2025) -- Sterilizing Filtration of Liquids | p56 - p70

    

### 本章學習目標

    

        
- 理解完整性測試 (Integrity Test) 的物理原理：擴散流量 (Diffusive Flow) 與泡點 (Bubble Point) 的基本機制

        
- 掌握完整性測試結果與細菌截留 (Bacterial Retention) 之間的關聯性，以及如何建立測試規格

        
- 學會根據濾膜面積選擇適當的測試方法（泡點法、擴散流量法、壓力保持法），並理解產品潤濕測試的轉換公式

        
- 了解 PUPSIT（使用前滅菌後完整性測試）的考量因素與法規期望

        
- 掌握完整性測試失敗的故障排除流程與潤濕不足的分析方法

    

7.0 Integrity Testing -- Overview 完整性測試概述

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Bacterial retention studies are used for validating a filter membrane but are not feasible for routine confirmation of the retentive capabilities of each filter used in the manufacture of sterile pharmaceuticals. Such challenge tests can clearly not be performed prior to the use of the filter in the production setting, as it involves deliberate introduction of contaminating microorganisms to the filter (a "destructive" test). It is also not feasible post-use, as it requires advanced microbiology equipment and multiday incubation periods. Hence the need for a nondestructive, physical-integrity test method that can be correlated with bacterial retention (i.e., can be used as a surrogate method for direct bacterial retention). The main objective of a nondestructive physical integrity test is to determine the presence of defects that may compromise a filter's retention capability without rendering the filter useless. Additionally, the integrity test establishes the similarity of the test filter to validated bacterial retention-challenged filters under process-related conditions.

        

For integrity tests on hydrophilic membranes, gas flow properties of wetted filter membranes are evaluated over a range of pressures. This can be demonstrated by completely wetting the entire filter membrane and introducing gas to the upstream side of the membrane at a low pressure. Capillary forces within the filter material keep the liquid from being expelled from the pores, and the wetted membrane functions as a barrier to convective gas flow. As this pressure is applied on the upstream side of the filter, a small amount of the gas dissolves into the wetting liquid, diffuses across the wetted membrane, and is released on the downstream side when it is maintained at atmospheric pressure (Figure 7.0-1). The diffusion rate increases as the pressure on the upstream side is increased. Once a critical pressure is achieved ("the bubble point"), the effect of capillary forces keeping the liquid in the pores will be overcome by sufficient pressure, pushing the wetting liquid out through the membrane pores. This happens first for the largest pores, where capillary forces are the weakest (Figure 7.0-2). If the rate of gas flow that passes to the downstream is measured at increasing pressure values, the membrane characterization curve (Figure 7.0-3) can be obtained for the given membrane filter.

        

Characterization of these dynamics (both the diffusive flow rate at pressures below the bubble point, as well as the exact bubble point pressure) can indicate integrity of the filter in a nondestructive manner, resulting in a method that can be performed on every filter used in production. Diffusive flow theory is discussed further in Section 10.1. Figure 7.0-1 illustrates gas diffusion through the wetted membrane pores at pressures where the wetting fluid is held in the pores by capillary forces. Figure 7.0-2 illustrates gas flow through the membrane at a pressure exceeding the bubble point where the wetting fluid is expelled from the largest pores.

        

*[Figure 7.0-1 Gas Diffusion Through a Wetted Membrane]*

        

*[Figure 7.0-2 Bubble Point Through a Wetted Membrane]*

        

Figure 7.0-3 illustrates the relationship between measured air flow downstream of a wetted filter membrane. Three characteristic portions of the curves act as the basis for membrane-filter integrity-testing:

        

            
1. The linear portion on the low end of the pressure axis shows diffusive gas flow through the liquid held in the pores of the membrane.

            
2. As the pressure is increased, there is a characteristic bend in the curve followed by another linear portion. This bend indicates the transition between diffusive gas flow and bulk, or viscous, flow.

            
3. For an integral filter, bulk gas flow occurs after the bubble point of the largest pores has been exceeded. Before reaching this point, the majority of gas flow is due to free-flowing gas through open pores; a minor portion of the flow results from diffusion through the pores of the membrane that are still wetted.

        

        

*[Figure 7.0-3 Characteristic Curve of the Membrane]*

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Integrity Test（完整性測試）：**一種非破壞性的物理測試方法，用來確認除菌濾膜在使用前後是否完好無損。由於細菌截留試驗 (Bacterial Retention Test) 是破壞性的，無法在每次生產時執行，因此需要一個「替代方法」來間接確認濾膜的截留能力。

            

**Bubble Point（泡點）：**當施加在濕潤濾膜上游的氣體壓力達到某個臨界值時，毛細管力不足以將液體保持在孔隙中，液體被推出最大孔隙，氣體開始大量通過。這個臨界壓力就是泡點。

            

**Diffusive Flow（擴散流量）：**在泡點以下的壓力下，少量氣體溶解進入潤濕液，擴散穿過濕潤的濾膜，在下游釋放出來。這個流量與濾膜完整性直接相關。

            

**Capillary Forces（毛細管力）：**液體在微小孔隙中因表面張力而產生的保持力。孔隙越小，毛細管力越大，需要越高的壓力才能將液體推出。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

**出門前檢查瓦斯：**想像你每天出門前都要確認瓦斯已經關好。你不可能每次都請瓦斯公司來做全面管線壓力測試（那就像細菌截留試驗，費時費力且具破壞性）。取而代之的是，你用簡單的方式——聞一聞有沒有瓦斯味、看看爐頭火焰是否正常——這就是「非破壞性完整性測試」的概念。

            

**吹氣球找漏洞：**泡點測試就像吹一個氣球——當壓力不大時，氣球表面的微小孔洞讓少量空氣慢慢滲出（擴散流量）。但當你用力吹到某個程度，最大的孔洞會突然讓大量空氣衝出來（泡點）。如果氣球在很低的壓力就大量漏氣，代表它有大洞（濾膜不完整）。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**為什麼完整性測試如此重要？**在除菌過濾的決策層級中，「無菌濾液保證」永遠是第一優先。完整性測試是連接「濾膜資格確認」與「實際生產使用」之間的橋樑——它讓我們能在不破壞濾膜的情況下，確認每一支生產用濾膜都具備與經過細菌截留驗證的濾膜相同的品質。

            

膜特性曲線 (Characteristic Curve) 的三個區域是理解所有完整性測試方法的基礎：低壓區（擴散流量）、轉折區、高壓區（泡點後的體積流量）。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 環境中，每個批次的除菌過濾都需要完整性測試。假設你的工廠一年生產 200 批無菌注射劑，每批都需要至少一次使用後完整性測試。如果其中一批測試失敗，可能意味著整批產品需要丟棄或返工——數百萬元的直接損失，還不包括調查成本和客戶信任的影響。理解完整性測試的物理原理，能幫助你正確解讀結果、區分真正的濾膜損壞與「假陽性失敗」。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼細菌截留試驗不適合作為每批生產的常規測試？請列出至少兩個原因。

                
2. 如果一支濾膜的泡點值異常偏低，這在物理上代表什麼意義？對無菌保證有何影響？

                
3. 膜特性曲線上的三個區域分別對應哪些完整性測試方法？

            

        

    

7.1 Relationship Between Integrity Test Results and Bacterial Retention 完整性測試結果與細菌截留的關係

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

During membrane development by the filter manufacturer, retentive capability can be assessed by challenging successively "tighter" samples of the specific membrane under standardized test conditions and analyzing the bacterial passage results. Typically, the retention pattern observed will allow identification of physical integrity-test specifications using standard wetting fluids--acceptance criteria for the measured parameters within which no bacterial penetration will occur under standardized testing conditions (6). The integrity-test value established by this exercise is linked to the sterility of the filtrate. Such establishment of integrity-test value specifications should incorporate a safety margin to account for natural variability in measurement and membrane manufacture (e.g., by applying appropriate statistics with confidence intervals).

        

*[Figure 7.1-1 Gas Flow Profile Values and Filtrate Sterility]*

        

Figure 7.1-1 illustrates a typical relationship between the gas flow profile values and filtrate sterility from a series of five filters with decreasing maximum pore size (from left to right).

        

The bubble point test relates to the effective diameter of the largest pores present in the membrane, and these pores, along with membrane thickness and pore tortuosity, directly influence the retention properties of the membrane. The resolution of the bubble point test diminishes as a function of increasing filter area, since diffusive gas flow below the bubble point tends to obscure it (41-43).

        

While diffusion does not bear a direct relationship to pore size, the diffusive flow test provides a quantitative measurement in which maximum flow limit is established by the filter manufacturer at a designated test pressure lower than the minimum bubble point value.

        

During membrane development and initial integrity-test qualification by the filter manufacturer, testing flow rate at multiple pressure values enables plotting of the gas flow curve from diffusion at low pressures through the bubble point region at elevated pressures. These tests combine the advantages of the bubble-point and single-point diffusive-flow integrity tests in characterizing the pore size distribution. Methods for mathematically characterizing the diffusive-flow to bulk-flow transition region and correlation of the value generated to bacterial titer reduction may be found in reference literature.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**完整性測試規格的建立：**濾膜製造商在開發階段會測試一系列「孔徑越來越緊」的濾膜樣品。對每個樣品同時進行細菌截留試驗和物理完整性測試，找出「完整性測試值」與「是否能完全截留細菌」之間的對應關係。最終設定的規格值會加入安全裕度 (Safety Margin)，以涵蓋量測和製造的自然變異。

            

**泡點 vs 擴散流量的互補性：**

            

                
- **Bubble Point（泡點）：**反映最大孔徑的有效直徑，是「最差情況」的指標

                
- **Diffusive Flow（擴散流量）：**反映整體膜結構的完整性，是一個定量的「綜合指標」

                
- 兩者結合可以更完整地描繪孔徑分佈 (Pore Size Distribution)

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

**駕照考試的及格線：**濾膜製造商建立完整性測試規格的過程，就像交通部門制定駕照考試標準。他們讓不同程度的駕駛（不同孔徑的濾膜）參加路考（細菌截留試驗），找出「筆試分數」（完整性測試值）和「實際駕駛安全」（能否截留細菌）之間的關聯。最後設定一個「及格線」（規格值），而且會比真正的臨界點稍微嚴格一些（安全裕度），確保所有通過的人都真的安全。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**泡點測試在大面積濾膜上的局限性：**隨著濾膜面積增加，泡點以下的擴散流量也會增加（因為擴散流量與面積成正比），這會「遮蔽」泡點的訊號，使泡點判定變得困難。這就是為什麼大面積濾膜通常使用擴散流量法而非泡點法。

            

**安全裕度的重要性：**規格值不是「剛好能截留細菌」的臨界值，而是加入了統計信賴區間的安全值。這體現了決策層級的第一原則：無菌濾液保證永遠優先於效率考量。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼完整性測試規格需要包含安全裕度？如果不加安全裕度會有什麼風險？

                
2. 為什麼泡點測試的解析度會隨著濾膜面積增加而降低？從物理原理的角度解釋。

                
3. 濾膜製造商如何將完整性測試值與細菌截留能力關聯起來？這個過程的關鍵步驟是什麼？

            

        

    

7.1.1 Test Method Selection 測試方法選擇

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

The method for integrity-testing of production filters by the filter user should be chosen to provide reliable results based on the nature of the filter, product, and processing conditions. Bubble point, multiple-point and single-point diffusive-flow and pressure-hold tests can be used, recognizing that each has strengths and limitations that must be evaluated in terms of the particular circumstances of the test. These test methods can be used for both hydrophilic and hydrophobic membrane filters and can be performed manually or preferentially with automated integrity-test instruments. Section 10.2 contains further discussion of filter integrity-test methods.

        

The flow rate of the test gas that passes through the wetting fluid in the pores of the filter media via diffusive flow is much lower than the flow rate of bulk gas that passes through the filter media when the wetting fluid is displaced from the larger pores of the filter media (i.e., what occurs at and above the bubble point). The rate at which test gas passes through the filter media via diffusive flow is directly related to the surface area of the filter media (i.e., as the filter surface area increases, the flow rate due to diffusive flow increases).

        

Integrity-test instruments have a lower limit at which they can reliably determine the flow rate of the test gas passing through the filter media. For this reason, there is typically a minimum value for the surface area of the filter being integrity-tested to perform a diffusive-flow integrity test. Below this minimum surface area, the automated integrity tester may not be capable of determining the diffusive flow at the specific test pressure (i.e., <= 80% of bubble point). In contrast, when using the bubble point method, the algorithm is looking at the change in the flow rate instead of the absolute flow rate as the differential pressure is increased (specifically, the pressure at which bulk flow starts). For this reason, the bubble point integrity-test method is typically used instead of the diffusive-flow integrity-test method to perform an integrity test on a filter with a small surface area.

        

Above the minimum surface-area threshold for testing via the diffusive-flow integrity-test method, either the diffusive-flow or the bubble point test method may be used for a range of filter surface areas. As the surface area of the filter media being tested increases significantly (e.g., in the case where multiple round housings are used), there comes a point where the diffusive flow of gas passing through the wetted membrane is so high that it will be difficult for the integrity test to distinguish the bubble point from the high rate of "background" diffusive flow through wetted pores. For this reason, the diffusive-flow method is typically selected for the largest filter sizes.

        

The exact cutoffs for small, medium, and large surface area depend upon the attributes of the filter media being tested, the wetting fluid used, and the capability of the automated integrity tester being used, but general guidance is provided in Table 7.1.1-1.

        
            Table 7.1.1-1 Suggested Integrity Test Methods Based on Filtration Surface Area
            
| Surface Area of Filter Media* | Suggested Integrity Test Method |
| --- | --- |
            
| < 0.03 m² | Bubble Point |
            
| 0.03 -- 1.8 m² | Bubble Point or Diffusive Flow |
            
| > 1.8 m² | Combination of Diffusive Flow and Bubble Point |
        

        

**These values are approximate values only. Consult Filter Manufacturer for specific guidance.*

        

One approach to diffusive-flow testing of large filter systems with multiple cartridges is to derive an assembly-specific value that is lower than the linear multiplied-limit of each cartridge. A technical evaluation should be conducted to justify this approach. If the assembly's diffusive air flow exceeds the corrected limit, an investigation would be required (e.g., individual tests on each cartridge, and confirmation of the seals with the housing).

        

When performing tests on filter capsules with associated SUS, the high pressures required for bubble point testing could exceed the pressure ratings of such equipment. For this reason, diffusive-flow tests may be preferred as they typically require lower pressures than bubble point-test methods. Or, in case the bubble point method is required, the SUS is designed to be compatible with a higher working-pressure range.

        

A modification to the diffusive flow method is a pressure-hold/decay method, where pressure is allowed to drop as diffusive flow across the wetted membrane occurs, instead of being held constant (see Appendix B for more information).

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**三種主要測試方法：**

            

                
- **Bubble Point（泡點法）：**量測最大孔隙被突破的壓力，適用於小面積濾膜

                
- **Diffusive Flow（擴散流量法）：**在泡點以下的壓力量測氣體擴散速率，適用於中大面積濾膜

                
- **Pressure Hold/Decay（壓力保持/衰減法）：**擴散流量法的變體，讓壓力自然下降來間接量測擴散流量

            

            

**面積與方法選擇的關係：**擴散流量與濾膜面積成正比。面積太小時，擴散流量低到儀器無法可靠量測，所以用泡點法。面積太大時，背景擴散流量太高會遮蔽泡點信號，所以用擴散流量法。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像你要檢查一面牆是否有裂縫：

            

                
- **小面牆（泡點法）：**你可以靠近仔細看，找到最大的裂縫在哪裡——容易判斷

                
- **大面牆（擴散流量法）：**牆面太大無法逐一檢查，但可以在牆的一側噴水霧，看另一側整體滲出了多少水——如果總滲水量在標準範圍內，代表牆面整體完好

                
- **超大面牆（壓力衰減法）：**你密封一個房間加壓，看壓力降多快來推算滲漏量

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**SUS 與壓力限制：**一次性使用系統 (Single-Use System, SUS) 的壓力耐受度通常比不鏽鋼系統低。泡點測試需要的壓力往往高於擴散流量測試，因此在 SUS 環境中，擴散流量法更為常用。如果硬要在 SUS 上執行泡點測試，可能會損壞管路或接頭。

            

**多濾芯組合的特殊處理：**當多支濾芯安裝在同一個外殼中時，擴散流量的上限不能簡單地將單支濾芯的限值乘以數量。需要建立「組合體專屬」的規格值，通常會低於線性倍數值。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 中，你可能同時處理不同客戶的產品。根據 Table 7.1.1-1 的指引：

            

                
- 實驗室小型濾膜（< 0.03 m²）：只用泡點法

                
- 標準 10 吋濾芯（~0.5-0.7 m²）：泡點或擴散流量皆可

                
- 多濾芯組合（> 1.8 m²）：以擴散流量為主，輔以泡點

            

            

在制定 SOP 時，應與濾膜供應商確認各濾膜型號的具體面積門檻值。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼小面積濾膜不適合用擴散流量法？請從儀器靈敏度的角度解釋。

                
2. 為什麼大面積濾膜不適合用泡點法？請從信噪比的角度解釋。

                
3. 如果你的製程使用 SUS 搭配除菌濾膜，在選擇完整性測試方法時需要額外考慮什麼因素？

            

        

    

7.1.2 Filtrate Sterility Assurance 濾液無菌保證

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Integrity-testing of sterilizing-grade production filters is a fundamental element of sterility assurance for the most critical applications that require a sterile claim (9, 11). However, integrity-testing alone is insufficient to ensure the sterility of the filtrate. Other control elements should also be in place, such as:

        

            
- Filter manufacturer's production controls and quality assurance systems should be in place to ensure the quality and uniformity of the filter membranes and fabricated filters.

            
- Filter user should conduct bacterial retention validation studies to demonstrate that product, processing conditions, and sterilizing-grade filter can effectively sterilize the fluid.

            
- Filter user should ensure appropriate product and process controls (e.g., system design, operating parameters, bioburden control, process monitoring) are in place so that the filtration operates within the validated parameters defined by the bacterial retention study.

        

        

With the appropriate controls in place, the filter integrity test is only one part of the overall sterility-assurance strategy. It is incumbent on the filter user to ensure that all elements are, and continue to remain, in place.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**完整性測試不等於無菌保證的全部：**完整的無菌保證策略需要三個層面的控制同時到位：

            

                
1. **濾膜製造商的品質控制：**確保每一批濾膜的品質和一致性

                
2. **用戶的驗證研究：**用特定產品和製程條件證明濾膜能有效除菌

                
3. **用戶的製程控制：**確保實際操作在驗證過的參數範圍內運行

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

**機場的多層安全機制：**完整性測試就像機場安檢門（金屬探測器）。但機場安全不僅僅靠安檢門——還需要行李 X 光機（生物負荷控制）、護照查驗（驗證研究）、以及航空公司的標準作業程序（製程控制）。任何一個環節的缺失都會危及整體安全，即使安檢門運作正常。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

這裡再次強調了無菌濾液保證 (Sterile Filtrate Assurance) 作為最高優先的原則。完整性測試通過只代表濾膜本身完好，但如果生物負荷 (Bioburden) 超出驗證範圍，或操作參數偏離驗證條件，濾液的無菌性仍然可能受到威脅。

            

                

1. 無菌濾液保證 Sterile Filtrate Assurance

                

▼

                

2. 產品品質 / CQAs

                

▼

                

3. 製程穩健性與商業效率

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 列舉三個即使完整性測試通過，濾液仍可能不無菌的情境。

                
2. 作為 CDMO 的營運主管，你如何確保無菌保證策略的「所有要素都持續到位」？

            

        

    

7.2 Automated Integrity-Test Instruments 自動化完整性測試儀器

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

The standard for modern filter integrity-testing utilizes automated integrity-test units, which provide the most reproducible and sensitive methods. Automated integrity-testers employ highly sensitive pressure sensors and/or gas flow meters, in combination with the careful regulation of pressure, to test filters in a highly repeatable manner.

        

Historically, filter integrity-testing had been performed manually via a combination of manual manipulation of pressure regulators, graduated cylinders, and/or visual detection of increasing gas flow rate via a stream of bubbles. Some manual integrity-test methods require downstream manipulations that could compromise the sterility of the system if performed before use. Automated integrity-test instruments perform the integrity test from the upstream (nonsterile) side of the filters, minimizing the risk for downstream contamination. Manual integrity-testing should now only be performed on production filters in special and justified cases, due to the ready availability of automated integrity-test instruments.

        

Automatic integrity-test equipment, both hardware and software, should be qualified, as described in Section 7.3. Most automated integrity-test instruments function by measuring pressure only upstream of the filter membrane, and assuming downstream pressure is atmospheric. Care must be taken if the downstream side of the membrane is not in equilibrium with the atmosphere.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Automated Integrity-Test Instruments（自動化完整性測試儀器）：**現代除菌過濾的標準是使用自動化儀器進行完整性測試。這些儀器使用高靈敏度的壓力感測器和/或氣體流量計，配合精確的壓力調節，提供高度可重複的測試結果。

            

**上游測試 vs 下游測試：**自動化儀器從濾膜的上游（非無菌側）進行測試，避免了手動方法需要在下游（無菌側）操作的風險。這是自動化儀器的一個關鍵優勢——不會破壞已建立的無菌狀態。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

手動完整性測試就像用肉眼和經驗判斷一個輪胎是否漏氣——你把輪胎泡在水裡，觀察有沒有氣泡冒出來。這種方法受限於觀察者的主觀判斷。自動化儀器則像是汽車維修廠的電子胎壓偵測系統——精確到毫巴等級，而且每次測量結果一致可追溯。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**手動測試的限制：**手動完整性測試「現在只應在特殊且有正當理由的情況下」對生產用濾膜執行。這反映了法規對資料完整性 (Data Integrity) 和可重現性的日益重視。在稽核中，如果被發現仍在使用手動方法而沒有充分的理由，可能會引發觀察缺失。

            

**下游壓力假設：**大多數自動化儀器假設下游壓力等於大氣壓。如果下游側未與大氣平衡（例如封閉的系統），測試結果可能不準確。這是一個實務上常被忽略的細節。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼自動化完整性測試儀器比手動方法更受法規青睞？請從再現性和資料完整性兩個角度說明。

                
2. 在什麼情況下，自動化儀器假設下游壓力為大氣壓的前提可能不成立？這會如何影響測試結果？

            

        

    

7.3 Qualification of Integrity Test Devices 完整性測試設備的確認

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Qualification of integrity-test devices is similar to qualifying other process test-equipment. Qualification of an integrity-test device begins with the development of the device and is usually conducted by the device manufacturer. Design qualification and device development documentation are generally generated by the device manufacturer. These documents may be included in the filter user's qualification documentation package. Equipment qualification should cover the key functions of the device; however, it may not cover all possible combinations of functions and configurations. Risk assessment, therefore, should include key functions such as, but not limited to:

        

            
- Test procedures as a main function of the device

            
- Detection of error conditions and messages

            
- Compliance with data integrity requirements and good documentation practices

            
- Qualification of the measurement itself (accuracy and limits)

        

        

Typical qualification activities may include:

        

            
- Computer software evaluation--test parameters, test methods, programming the unit, and tests (e.g., ease of use, test options, networking capability, operating systems)

            
- Unit sensitivity evaluation

            
- Unit startup

            
- Unit calibration

            
- Performing the tests

            
- Integrity-test performance evaluation (bubble point, diffusive flow, pressure hold)

            
- Test other functions (volume determination, failure modes, ejecting invalid entries)

            
- Test printout evaluation

            
- Password protection in combination with appropriate user roles and permission levels to avoid modification of a test program by an unauthorized user.

            
- Peripheral function evaluation (date/time clock, memory, cleaning)

        

        

Integrity-test devices that measure pressure and/or gas flow should be calibrated using relevant calibration standards and should generate records according to applicable regulatory expectations.

        

Automated integrity-testers often incorporate sensitivity settings and test algorithms to detect atypical test conditions and to reliably test different filter sizes. These sensitivity settings are of importance and require careful observation to assure the right sensitivity for the particular filter-size is chosen, otherwise the integrity test may lack accuracy and validity. The sensitivity parameter establishment can be performed or confirmed during process qualification (PQ). For thorough qualification strategy, end users should consider confirming not only that the unit can successfully return a "pass" integrity result for integral filters but can also reliably detect broken filters or incorrect test setups.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**設備確認 (Equipment Qualification)：**完整性測試儀器的確認遵循與其他製程測試設備相同的原則——DQ（設計確認）、IQ（安裝確認）、OQ（操作確認）、PQ（性能確認）。設備製造商通常負責 DQ 和部分 OQ，終端用戶負責確認設備在實際使用條件下的表現。

            

**Sensitivity Settings（靈敏度設定）：**自動化儀器會根據不同的濾膜尺寸調整靈敏度。選錯靈敏度可能導致測試結果不準確——太靈敏會產生假失敗，不夠靈敏則可能讓真正有缺陷的濾膜通過。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

確認完整性測試儀器就像校準一台體溫計。你不僅要確認它在正常體溫（36.5 度C）時讀數正確（能判定「健康」），還要確認它在發燒溫度（38 度C以上）時也能準確讀出（能偵測到「異常」）。如果你只驗證了「正常通過」的情境，卻沒有驗證「應該失敗」的情境，那這台儀器的確認就不完整。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**資料完整性 (Data Integrity) 是關鍵：**現代法規對電子記錄的要求越來越嚴格。完整性測試儀器必須滿足：密碼保護、使用者權限分級、審計追蹤 (Audit Trail)、以及防止未授權修改測試程式。這些都是稽核的重點項目。

            

**「通過」和「失敗」都要確認：**完整的確認策略不僅要確認儀器能讓完好的濾膜「通過」，還要能可靠地偵測到破損的濾膜或不正確的測試設定。這是很多工廠容易忽略的地方。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 在完整性測試儀器的確認過程中，為什麼必須同時驗證「通過」和「失敗」兩種情境？

                
2. 如果靈敏度設定與實際使用的濾膜尺寸不匹配，可能會產生哪些問題？

                
3. 從資料完整性的角度，列舉至少三個完整性測試儀器必須具備的功能。

            

        

    

7.4 Product Wet Integrity Tests 產品潤濕完整性測試

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

The default "reference" wetting fluid for physical integrity tests of hydrophilic filters, as validated by membrane manufacturers, is typically water. However, for testing production filters, drug product or buffers may be the most appropriate wetting fluid (e.g., after use, when the filter is already wetted with this fluid). A new integrity-test specification, customized for the unique wetting fluid, can be determined during filter validation by executing a protocol in which the reference fluid specification is "converted" to an appropriate specification for the new wetting fluid. This specification is then, by extension, also correlated to the bacterial retention capabilities of the membrane.

        

Differences between product-wetted integrity test values and reference fluid-wetted integrity test values are due to differences in test gas solubility, the diffusion constant, and the surface tension of the wetting fluid.

        

The scale-down studies are used to determine the correction factor between the water-wet integrity-test specification and the required product-wet test limits.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Product-Wet vs Water-Wet（產品潤濕 vs 水潤濕）：**濾膜製造商提供的完整性測試規格通常以水作為標準潤濕液。但在實際生產中，濾膜在使用後已經被藥品溶液潤濕。由於藥品的表面張力、氣體溶解度和擴散係數與水不同，完整性測試的數值也會不同。因此需要進行「轉換」，建立產品潤濕的專屬規格。

            

**影響測試值差異的三個因素：**

            

                
- **Test gas solubility（測試氣體溶解度）：**氣體在產品中的溶解度可能與水不同

                
- **Diffusion constant（擴散常數）：**氣體穿過潤濕液的擴散速率不同

                
- **Surface tension（表面張力）：**直接影響泡點壓力

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

**泡茶時茶葉釋出物 vs 實際喝到的：**想像你用同一個茶壺泡不同的茶——綠茶和紅茶的滲出速率不同，顏色深淺也不同。同樣地，用水潤濕和用藥品潤濕的濾膜，在完整性測試中的表現也不同。你不能用「綠茶的標準」去判斷「紅茶是否泡好了」——需要針對每種茶（潤濕液）建立各自的標準。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Scale-Down Studies 的重要性：**轉換係數的建立通常在小規模實驗中完成，使用濾膜碟片 (Filter Discs) 而非全尺寸的濾芯。這是因為碟片更容易操控和乾燥，可以在相同的濾膜上依序測試水潤濕和產品潤濕的差異。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼在生產環境中，產品潤濕測試比水潤濕測試更具實際意義？

                
2. 如果藥品的表面張力低於水，你預期泡點值會如何變化？為什麼？

            

        

    

7.4.1 Product-Wetted Bubble Point Tests 產品潤濕泡點測試

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Tests for determination of product-wet bubble point limits should be conducted, first with water followed by product-wetting and then by the product-wet test. The technical rationale for establishment of product-wet bubble point values should be documented. Bubble point values are affected by the surface tension and temperature of the wetting fluid. Section 7.4.1.1 describes one method used to establish bubble point specifications using filter discs. Other methods may be appropriate if scientifically justified (see Section 10.2 for further discussion of bubble point tests).

        

### 7.4.1.1 Bubble Point Ratio Approach

        

For determining product-specific bubble point specifications, testing can generally be conducted as follows:

        

            
1. Select multiple samples of filter discs for testing--generally at least three membrane lots. Since the bubble point refers to specific values relating to the membrane's pore size and the wetting-liquid surface tension, filter discs can be used.

            
2. Install the membrane discs in the holder and rinse them with the reference wetting liquid (e.g., water, alcohol).

            
3. Perform the bubble point test on each disc.

            
4. Either completely dry the filter discs or rinse the membranes with an appropriate amount of the product in question to ensure complete removal of the wetting fluid used in the first integrity test.

            
5. Perform the bubble point test with the product. These values are used to calculate the product-wet bubble point limit.

        

        

The bubble point limit for product can be calculated using the formula given in Equation 1. This example uses water as the reference fluid, which correlates the product-wetted-filter bubble point test data to the minimum water-wetted bubble point value given by the filter manufacturer.

        

            **Equation 1:**  

            PBPmin = WBPmin x (PBPavg / WBPavg)  
  

            Where:  

            PBPmin = Product-wetted bubble point, minimum (minimum validated product-wetted bubble point)  

            WBPmin = Water-wetted bubble point, minimum (minimum water-wetted bubble point specified by the filter supplier)  

            PBPavg = Average product-wetted bubble point of the test samples recorded in the test  

            WBPavg = Average water-wetted bubble point of the test samples recorded in the test
        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Bubble Point Ratio Approach（泡點比值法）：**這是一種將水潤濕泡點規格「轉換」為產品潤濕泡點規格的標準方法。核心邏輯是：產品潤濕泡點與水潤濕泡點之間存在一個穩定的比例關係（主要由表面張力決定），這個比例可以從小規模實驗中測定，然後應用到製造商提供的水潤濕最低泡點值上。

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Formula

            

```

Equation 1: Product-Wetted Bubble Point Minimum

PBP_min = WBP_min x (PBP_avg / WBP_avg)

範例計算：
假設：
  WBP_min (供應商規格) = 3200 mbar
  WBP_avg (水潤濕實測平均) = 3800 mbar
  PBP_avg (產品潤濕實測平均) = 3040 mbar

則：比值 = PBP_avg / WBP_avg = 3040 / 3800 = 0.80

PBP_min = 3200 x 0.80 = 2560 mbar

意義：產品潤濕的最低泡點規格為 2560 mbar
            
```

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

這就像匯率轉換。濾膜製造商給你的是「美元價格」（水潤濕泡點規格），但你的工廠使用「歐元」（產品潤濕）。你需要找出匯率（比值），然後把美元價格轉換成歐元價格。匯率的計算方式是：用同一批濾膜碟片，分別量測「美元」和「歐元」的數值，算出比例。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**至少三個膜批次：**測試必須使用至少三個不同的濾膜批次，以確保比值具有統計代表性。只用一個批次的數據可能無法反映批次間的正常變異。

            

**完全去除前一種潤濕液：**在從水潤濕切換到產品潤濕之前，必須確保水已被完全去除（乾燥或充分沖洗）。殘留的水會影響產品潤濕泡點的準確性。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果產品的表面張力是水的 80%，你預期 PBP_avg / WBP_avg 的比值大約是多少？

                
2. 為什麼測試需要至少三個不同的膜批次？只用一個批次有什麼風險？

                
3. 使用上述範例的數據，如果你工廠實測的產品潤濕泡點為 2400 mbar，這支濾膜是否通過測試？

            

        

    

7.4.2 Product-Wetted Diffusive Flow Test 產品潤濕擴散流量測試

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

The determination of product-wetted test specifications for diffusive flow is a two-step process, which requires first, identifying the bubble point ratio as described in Equation 1.

        

**Step 1: Determination of Test Pressure**

        

The test pressure for the product-wetted diffusive flow test is typically calculated using the following formula and the determined product wet bubble point values:

        

            **Equation 2:**  

            TPPW = MTPWW x (PBPavg / WBPavg)  
  

            Where:  

            TPPW = Test pressure, product-wetted (varies with surface tension)  

            MTPWW = Manufacturer test pressure, water-wetted (or other test solvent) (see Section 10.2)  

            PBPavg = Average product-wetted bubble point of the test samples recorded in the test  

            WBPavg = Average water-wetted bubble point of the test samples recorded in the test
        

        

**Step 2: Determination of the Product-Wetted Diffusive Flow Limit**

        

The product-wetted diffusive-flow limit is then typically determined as follows:

        

            
1. Conduct replicate water-wetted diffusive-flow tests on the filter assembly at the test pressure specified by the filter manufacturer (small-scale devices may be used as long as an accurate determination of flow is possible).

            
2. Dry the previously water-wet tested filter assembly and conduct several replicates of the product-wetted diffusive-flow test at the appropriate test pressure determined in Step 1, Equation 2 above.

            
3. Calculate the diffusive-flow test limit using the formula expressed in Equation 3:

        

        

            **Equation 3:**  

            DFLPW = DFLWW x (DFPW / DFWW)  
  

            Where:  

            DFLPW = Diffusive flow limit, product-wetted  

            DFLWW = Diffusive-flow test limit specified by the supplier, water-wetted  

            DFPW = Diffusive flow, product-wetted  

            DFWW = Diffusive flow, water-wetted
        

        

Diffusion values are affected by the solubility of the test gas in the wetting fluid and its diffusion constant through the wetting fluid, therefore acceptance criteria are specific to a particular test gas being used.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**兩步驟轉換流程：**產品潤濕的擴散流量規格建立比泡點更複雜，需要兩個步驟：

            

                
1. **Step 1 -- 轉換測試壓力：**使用與泡點相同的比值，將水潤濕的測試壓力轉換為產品潤濕的測試壓力

                
2. **Step 2 -- 轉換擴散流量限值：**在新的測試壓力下，比較水潤濕和產品潤濕的擴散流量，算出轉換係數

            

        

        

            

#### 公式與計算 Formula

            

```

Step 1: 測試壓力轉換 (Equation 2)
TP_PW = MTP_WW x (PBP_avg / WBP_avg)

範例：
  MTP_WW = 2500 mbar (供應商指定)
  比值 = 0.80 (從 Equation 1 計算)
  TP_PW = 2500 x 0.80 = 2000 mbar

Step 2: 擴散流量限值轉換 (Equation 3)
DFL_PW = DFL_WW x (DF_PW / DF_WW)

範例：
  DFL_WW = 12 ml/min (供應商規格)
  DF_WW = 8 ml/min (水潤濕實測)
  DF_PW = 10 ml/min (產品潤濕實測)
  DFL_PW = 12 x (10/8) = 15 ml/min
            
```

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**測試氣體的影響：**擴散流量的數值還受測試氣體種類影響。不同氣體在潤濕液中的溶解度和擴散係數不同，因此驗收標準必須針對特定的測試氣體。在實務中，壓縮空氣和氮氣是最常用的測試氣體，但兩者的擴散特性有差異——切換氣體時必須重新建立規格。

            

**為什麼產品潤濕的擴散流量可能高於水潤濕？**如果產品中測試氣體的溶解度較高或擴散係數較大，同一支完好濾膜的產品潤濕擴散流量會高於水潤濕值。因此，產品潤濕的限值 (DFL_PW) 通常也會高於水潤濕限值 (DFL_WW)。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼擴散流量的轉換需要兩個步驟，而不能像泡點那樣一步完成？

                
2. 如果你在驗證過程中切換了測試氣體（從壓縮空氣改為氮氣），是否需要重新建立產品潤濕規格？為什麼？

            

        

    

7.5 When a Sterilizing-Grade Filter Should be Integrity-Tested 除菌級濾膜應在何時進行完整性測試

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Where the claimed purpose of the filter is to sterilize, post-use integrity-testing is mandatory. This confirms that the filter remained integral throughout its use and was capable of retaining microorganisms. If truly nonintegral filters are detected post-use, a thorough investigation to determine the root cause is required. Guidance on best practice is to leverage the supplier's or manufacturer's expertise. In most cases, it also results in discarding a drug batch (or reprocessing, where validated) to protect patient safety from exposure to a nonsterile product.

        

For filters marketed for critical sterilizing filtration, each filter element should also be integrity-tested by the filter manufacturer prior to release.

        

Integrity-testing can also be performed by the end user prior to use, either before the filter itself is sterilized (when sterilized by the end user) or after sterilization (Figure 7.5-1). This allows early detection of nonintegral filters or improperly installed filters prior to execution of the filtration process. Whether to test filters in-line or off-line will depend on actual process requirements, but the test must include the cartridge already installed in the filter-housing (if applicable) so the seal between the filter element and the housing is also confirmed. Regulatory expectations regarding pre- and post-filtration integrity-testing may differ regionally (9, 11). In general, the objectives of pre- and post-filtration integrity-testing vary, and the need for each should be informed by risk assessment.

        

*[Figure 7.5-1 Filter Lifecycle -- Opportunities for Integrity-Testing]*

        

Pre-use, pre-sterilization integrity tests performed by the end user would be redundant to the integrity test performed by the filter manufacturer to release the sterilizing-grade filter from their production. However, a presterilization test will additionally confirm that an integral filter of the proper pore size has been correctly installed in the housing, and that damage has not occurred during shipping and handling. A post-sterilization integrity test provides the same information as a pre-sterilization test plus confirmation that the filter was not damaged during sterilization. Steps must be taken to ensure that the downstream side of the system remains sterile when performing PUPSIT.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**濾膜生命週期中的測試時機：**

            

                
- **製造商出廠測試：**每支除菌級濾膜在出廠前都經過完整性測試

                
- **用戶使用前、滅菌前測試：**確認安裝正確、運輸無損壞（與出廠測試重複）

                
- **用戶使用前、滅菌後測試 (PUPSIT)：**額外確認滅菌過程未損壞濾膜

                
- **用戶使用後測試（強制性）：**確認濾膜在整個使用過程中保持完整

            

            

**PUPSIT（使用前滅菌後完整性測試）：**在濾膜滅菌後、過濾產品之前進行的測試。必須確保下游系統的無菌狀態不被破壞。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

**出門前檢查瓦斯（再次強化）：**

            

                
- **出廠測試 = 瓦斯公司安裝後的驗收：**確認設備出廠合格

                
- **使用前測試 = 你自己聞一聞：**確認搬進新家後管線沒問題

                
- **PUPSIT = 每次用完瓦斯後確認關閉：**確認最近一次使用後一切正常

                
- **使用後測試 = 做完飯後的最終確認：**這是強制性的——必須確認瓦斯已安全關閉

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**使用後測試是強制性的：**如果濾膜的聲稱用途是除菌，使用後完整性測試是「mandatory（強制性的）」——沒有例外。如果測試失敗，通常意味著整批產品需要丟棄或返工。

            

**法規差異：**對於使用前測試（特別是 PUPSIT），不同地區的法規期望可能不同。EU GMP Annex 1 對 PUPSIT 有更明確的期望，而 FDA 的要求相對靈活。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼使用後完整性測試是「強制性的」而非「建議性的」？從病患安全的角度解釋。

                
2. 使用前滅菌前測試與出廠測試有何重疊？為什麼仍有其價值？

                
3. 執行 PUPSIT 時，「確保下游系統的無菌狀態不被破壞」具體需要哪些措施？

            

        

    

7.5.1 Pre-Use Post-Sterilization Integrity Test (PUPSIT) Considerations PUPSIT 考量

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

The post-use test is designed to detect any filter damage that occurred throughout its lifecycle, up to and including the filtration process itself. However, under extreme circumstances, post-filtration integrity test results may be influenced (i.e., shifted) by high-foulant fluids, which may mask a filter flaw or larger pore structure (44-47). In this scenario a PUPSIT result could identify filter flaws or filter damage when a post-use integrity may not. Recent publications have shown that these conditions are atypical for terminal filtration steps as filter-fouling is typically avoided within these filtration applications. Filterability studies, performed to determine the appropriate filter size and area before any filter design is established, will indicate the fluid-fouling propensity and filter flaw-masking risk, and gauge potential preventive measurements against any fouling (47).

        

In filtration applications with significant pore-plugging or large-pore structure-blockage potential, it is advisable to know the filter's prefiltration integrity-test value prior to the influences of contact with the full batch of product (or more strictly, the potential of foulants to shift the measured post-use integrity-test results in the direction that might cause false passes.) Any excessive fouling conditions would be also evidenced by significant flux decay or required pressure increase to maintain flow. True post-use integrity-test failures are typically a result of damages due to extreme mechanical or thermal process conditions. Such damages are typically catastrophic, and flaw-masking would not be possible for catastrophic or gross damage to filter membranes, as this damage is not capable of being "masked" by components of the fluid to an extent that allows a post-use test to appear to pass (48). However, in cases where significant fouling of the filter is possible, it could potentially mask rare marginal membrane flaws, which may not be detected by the post-use integrity test. Excessive filter-fouling could also be detected by special customizations to the post-use test, as the decrease in porosity and blockage of the largest pores would be manifested in a decrease in diffusive flow and in an increase in the bubble point, respectively (49). Alternative means also exist to detect any fouling that has the potential to modify post-use test value, including flow and differential-pressure monitoring during filtration, and possible modifications to the post-use test to detect unexpectedly low diffusive-flow values or unexpectedly high bubble points. Further, any risk of such flaw-masking (due to product-specific mechanisms of shifting the integrity-test results after fouling) can be evaluated during process design. Decades of experiences of filter suppliers and end-users showed that this type of behavior is scarce and evaluated during filterability tests respectively filter area sizing and process validation.

        

Any potential risks involved in the sterilizing filtration activity must be thoroughly assessed (28, 50, 51). While PUPSIT is a common regulatory expectation, there may be process constraints where it is not feasible (11). In such cases, and in relevant jurisdictions, a thorough risk assessment is required not to justify omission, but to evaluate and manage the risks associated with not performing PUPSIT. This includes assessing the filter sterilization process, supply chain controls, packaging, product characteristics, and pre-filtration steps. The goal of this assessment is to ensure that adequate controls are in place to mitigate the risk of using any non-integral filters.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Flaw-Masking（缺陷遮蔽）：**這是 PUPSIT 爭議的核心問題。在某些極端情況下，高堵塞性流體 (High-Foulant Fluids) 可能在使用後測試中「遮蔽」濾膜缺陷——堵塞的孔隙使得擴散流量降低、泡點升高，讓一支有缺陷的濾膜看起來像是通過了測試。PUPSIT 能在產品接觸前偵測到這些缺陷。

            

**但是——這種情況非常罕見：**文件明確指出，數十年的經驗顯示這種行為「is scarce（很稀少的）」。而且災難性損壞（如嚴重的機械或熱損傷）不可能被產品成分「遮蔽」到讓使用後測試通過的程度。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像你在檢查一個水管是否有裂縫。如果水管裡有很多水垢（fouling），水垢可能會堵住小裂縫，讓漏水測試看起來正常。這就是 flaw-masking。PUPSIT 就像是在水垢形成之前先測一次——確認水管本身是完好的。但實際上，如果水管有大的裂口（catastrophic damage），水垢不可能堵住它；只有微小的邊緣缺陷才可能被遮蔽。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**PUPSIT 不可行時的風險評估：**文件強調，不執行 PUPSIT 時需要的風險評估「不是為了合理化省略 (not to justify omission)」，而是為了「評估和管理相關風險」。這個措辭非常重要——法規並不接受「因為不方便所以不做」的理由，而是要求你證明有足夠的替代控制措施來降低風險。

            

**偵測堵塞的替代方法：**過濾過程中的流量和壓差監控、使用後測試的特殊客製化（偵測異常低的擴散流量或異常高的泡點）都是偵測堵塞的手段。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

作為 CDMO，你可能面臨客戶或法規要求執行 PUPSIT 的情境。評估時需考慮：

            

                
- 產品的堵塞傾向（透過 filterability studies 評估）

                
- SUS 是否能承受 PUPSIT 所需的壓力

                
- 下游無菌維護的可行性

                
- 是否有足夠的替代控制（如冗餘過濾、生物負荷監控）

            

            

如果決定不執行 PUPSIT，風險評估文件必須經過品質部門審核，並在法規稽核時隨時可供查閱。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 什麼是 flaw-masking？在什麼類型的產品中最可能發生？

                
2. 為什麼 catastrophic filter damage 不可能被 flaw-masking 遮蔽？

                
3. 如果你決定不執行 PUPSIT，風險評估中必須包含哪些要素？

            

        

    

7.5.2 Post-Filtration Integrity-Test Considerations 過濾後完整性測試考量

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

For operational reasons, the post-filtration integrity test should be accomplished as soon as feasible to avoid any detrimental test influences, for example, filter membrane wetting problems. Product residues should not dry out on the membrane and should be removed, if possible (by sufficiently flushing the filter with an appropriate fluid, post-use), if not testing in product. Filters should not be discarded until the integrity-test results are reviewed. Storage conditions and duration should be qualified to ensure they do not adversely affect the integrity of the filter. In cases of abnormally long delay between the use of the filter and its integrity test, the possibility of false passes should be evaluated.

        

The post-use test is not only a test of membrane integrity, but of the junction between the filter element and its housing or capsule. The filter element to be tested should therefore remain within the filter-housing to ensure that the filter and its junction with the housing has been integral throughout the filtration process. The post-use integrity test could be performed in-line or off-line within specific integrity-test laboratories within the end user's facility. The post-use test can be performed as a product-wet or water-wet procedure. Confirmation of integrity must be obtained before any product batch is released; therefore, the filter must not be discarded before the test result is obtained. If the filter receives an apparently failing integrity-test result, specific activities for retesting or root cause analysis are required and should be documented in the relevant procedure or batch record.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**使用後測試的實務要求：**

            

                
- **盡快執行：**避免產品殘留乾燥在膜上影響潤濕和測試結果

                
- **不要丟棄濾膜：**在測試結果確認前，濾膜必須保留——這是批次放行的前提條件

                
- **保持在外殼中：**測試的不僅是濾膜本身，還包括濾膜與外殼的密封接合

                
- **存儲條件需確認：**如果使用和測試之間有延遲，存儲條件和時間必須經過驗證

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

使用後完整性測試就像犯罪現場鑑識——必須在「現場」盡快完成（不要讓證據被破壞），而且必須保留「物證」（不要丟棄濾膜），直到「案件結案」（批次放行）。如果你把濾膜從外殼中取出再測試，就像是把證據從犯罪現場移走再分析——你無法確認它在原始位置的狀態。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**批次放行的門檻：**「確認完整性必須在任何產品批次放行之前獲得」——這是一個明確的法規期望。如果完整性測試結果是失敗的或可疑的，產品批次不能放行，必須進行調查。

            

**延遲測試的風險：**如果使用和測試之間的延遲異常長，必須評估「假通過」的可能性。產品殘留乾燥可能改變膜的潤濕特性，導致不準確的測試結果。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼使用後測試應「盡快」執行？延遲測試可能造成哪些問題？

                
2. 為什麼濾膜在測試前必須保持在外殼中？如果取出會遺漏什麼資訊？

            

        

    

7.5.3 Integrity Testing for Serial or Redundant Filtration 串聯或冗餘過濾的完整性測試

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

Manufacturing processes may be designed with trains of multiple filters, but the purpose of these extra filters varies from process to process (see Section 5.0). This purpose determines the need for integrity-testing of each filter. If one filter has been validated to achieve sterilization with a specific product, then the single sterilizing filter must satisfactorily pass integrity-testing after use.

        

### 7.5.3.1 Two-Filter Sterilization (Double Filtration)

        

In double filtration, the filter train is considered to be a sterilizing unit, and all sterilizing filters within the train must satisfactorily pass integrity-testing after use.

        

### 7.5.3.2 Pre-Filtration

        

For prefiltration, requirements for integrity-testing must be determined by the end user in an overall assessment during process design. Depending on the purpose of the filter, integrity-testing (correlated to complete bacterial retention) may not always be necessary.

        

### 7.5.3.3 Redundant Filtration

        

The primary filter (generally the farthest downstream) must be integrity-tested post-use. The secondary (redundant) sterilizing filter may not require post-use integrity-testing unless the primary sterilizing filter fails. In that case, the redundant filter must satisfactorily pass post-use integrity-testing and the reason for the failure of the primary filter should be investigated including confirmation of the sterile boundary. If the sterilizing-filtration process is redundant and registered as having PUPSIT, both filters should undergo PUPSIT for them to be considered comparable.

        

Performing PUPSIT on both filters in a redundant filtration configuration can be quite complex. Each filter must be tested individually after sufficient wetting; a single test cannot typically be used to test both filters simultaneously. Precautions should be taken to maintain the sterility of the fluid pathway between the two filters, as that region becomes critical for product sterility should the downstream filter fail, and the upstream filter is relied upon for sterility. Controls can include the use of additional sterilizing filters to vent the integrity-test gas from the upstream filter and introduce the test gas for integrity-testing the downstream filter. To test the downstream filter, there must be a valve or other closure between it and the upstream filter. In this type of setup, the integrity-test process-method development should include a risk assessment to ensure that the effects of wetting, or nonintegrity of the product and vent filters, does not interfere with the filter integrity-test result (52, 53). Further details on these considerations were discussed in PDA's Points to Consider for Implementation of Pre-Use Post-Sterilization Integrity Testing (PUPSIT).

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**三種多濾膜配置的測試要求：**

            

                
- **Double Filtration（雙重過濾）：**兩支濾膜都是除菌用途，都必須通過使用後測試

                
- **Pre-Filtration（預過濾）：**非除菌用途，完整性測試不一定需要（取決於用途）
